–ü–∞—Ä–∞–Ω–¥–∂–∞ ‚Äì –∂–µ–Ω—Å–∫–∞—è –≤–µ—Ä—Ö–Ω—è—è –æ–¥–µ–∂–¥–∞ –≤ –º—É—Å—É–ª—å–º–∞–Ω—Å–∫–∏—Ö —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∞—Ö, –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è—é—â–∞—è —Å–æ–±–æ–π —Ö–∞–ª–∞—Ç —Å –¥–ª–∏–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –ª–æ–∂–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Ä—É–∫–∞–≤–∞–º–∏ –∏ —Å –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞—é—â–µ–π –ª–∏—Ü–æ –≤–æ–ª–æ—Å—è–Ω–æ–π —Å–µ—Ç–∫–æ–π.] –æ–Ω–∏ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞—é—Ç –ø–∞–¥—à–∏–º–∏ –∏ –≥—Ä—è–∑–Ω—ã–º–∏. –û–Ω –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –∏–º–µ–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤ –∏–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–æ–∫, –Ω–æ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –µ—Å–ª–∏ –≤ –æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –æ–Ω–∏ –±—É–¥—É—Ç —Å–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞–Ω–Ω—ã –∏ —Å–∫—Ä–æ–º–Ω—ã. –û–Ω –æ–±–µ—â–∞–ª –≤–∑—è—Ç—å —Ç–µ–±—è –Ω–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É, –æ–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –ø—Ä–∏ —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏–∏, —á—Ç–æ —Ç—ã –Ω–∏–∫–æ–º—É –Ω–µ –±—É–¥–µ—à—å —Ä–∞—Å—Å–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ —Å–µ–±–µ –∏ —Å–≤–æ–µ–º –ø—Ä–æ—à–ª–æ–º, –ø–æ –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏—à—å —Å–≤–æ—é –≤–Ω–µ—à–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∏ –±—É–¥–µ—à—å –≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏ —Å–µ–±—è –æ—á–µ–Ω—å —Ç–∏—Ö–æ. –û–Ω –Ω–µ —Ö–æ—á–µ—Ç, –∞ —Ç–æ—á–Ω–µ–µ, –±–æ–∏—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º —Å –Ω–∞—à–µ–π —Ä–æ–¥–Ω–µ–π. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –±—É–¥–µ—à—å —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å, –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—à—å –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∏ —Å–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç—å –∂–∏–ª—å–µ, –∏ –∫–æ–ø–∏—Ç—å –¥–µ–Ω—å–≥–∏ –Ω–∞ –∞–¥–≤–æ–∫–∞—Ç–æ–≤. –ù–æ —Å–∞–º–æ–µ –≥–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ–µ ‚Äì —Ç—ã —Å–º–æ–∂–µ—à—å –≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å—Å—è —Å –ù–∞–¥–∏–º–æ–º! ‚Äì –ø–æ–¥–≤–µ–¥—è –∏—Ç–æ–≥, –≤–æ—Å–∫–ª–∏–∫–Ω—É–ª–∞ –ê–ª–∏—è –∏ –æ–±–ª–µ–≥—á–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –≤–∑–¥–æ—Ö–Ω—É–ª–∞.
–í—ã–π–¥—è –∏–∑ –±–æ–ª—å–Ω–∏—Ü—ã, –æ–Ω–∞ —Å–ø–æ–∫–æ–π–Ω–æ –≤–∑—è–ª–∞ –∏–∑ —Ä—É–∫ –ú—É—Ñ–∏–¥–∞ –∫–æ–Ω–≤–µ—Ä—Ç —Å –¥–µ–Ω—å–≥–∞–º–∏ –∏ –±–∏–ª–µ—Ç –Ω–∞ —Å–∞–º–æ–ª–µ—Ç. –û–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–æ –∞—ç—Ä–æ–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞ –∂–µ–Ω—â–∏–Ω–∞ –ø–æ–µ—Ö–∞–ª–∞ –≤ –≥–æ—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∏—Ü—É, —Ä–∞—Å–ø–æ–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—É—é –Ω–∞ —Ç–∏—Ö–æ–π —É–ª–æ—á–∫–µ –°—Ç–∞—Ä–æ–≥–æ –î–∞–º–∞—Å–∫–∞. –í—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—è —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è —Å–≤–æ–µ–≥–æ –±—É–¥—É—â–µ–≥–æ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª—å–Ω–∏–∫–∞, –ú–∞—Ä–∏–Ω–∞ –∫–∞—Ä–¥–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ
–∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–∞ –≤–Ω–µ—à–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å. –ò–∑ —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ–π –≥–æ–ª—É–±–æ–≥–ª–∞–∑–æ–π –±–ª–æ–Ω–¥–∏–Ω–∫–∏ –æ–Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –≤ –∂–≥—É—á—É—é –±—Ä—é–Ω–µ—Ç–∫—É —Å –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–º–∏ –∫–∞—Ä–∏–º–∏ –≥–ª–∞–∑–∞–º–∏ –∏ —Å–º—É–≥–ª—ã–º, –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –∑–∞–≥–æ—Ä–µ–ª—ã–º –ª–∏—Ü–æ–º. –ü—Ä–∏ –ø–æ–º–æ—â–∏ –∫—Ä–∞—Å–æ–∫, –∫–æ—Å–º–µ—Ç–∏–∫–∏ –∏ –≥–ª–∞–∑–Ω—ã—Ö –ª–∏–Ω–∑, –æ–±–ª–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –≤ –¥–ª–∏–Ω–Ω—É—é –ø–∞—Ä–∞–Ω–¥–∂—É, –æ–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∞–ª–∞ –ø–æ—Ö–æ–∂–∞ –Ω–∞ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç–æ—è—â—É—é –º—É—Å—É–ª—å–º–∞–Ω–∫—É.
‚Äì –ó–∞—á–µ–º? ‚Äì –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏–ª –ú—É—Ñ–∏–¥ –∏ –∑–∞–¥—É–º—á–∏–≤–æ –∑–∞–º–æ–ª—á–∞–ª. ‚Äì –Ø –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ–µ –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª. –Ø –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª, –∫–∞–∫ –≤–∏–Ω–æ–≤–∞—Ç –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ —Ç–æ–±–æ–π. –°–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —è –±—ã–ª —Å—á–∞—Å—Ç–ª–∏–≤. –Ø –∫—É–ø–∞–ª—Å—è –≤ —Å–≤–æ–µ–º –≤–µ–ª–∏—á–∏–∏, –∫—É–ø–∞–ª—Å—è –≤ –±–æ–≥–∞—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ –∏ –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏, —Å–≤–∞–ª–∏–≤—à–∏—Ö—Å—è –Ω–∞ –º–µ–Ω—è –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ —Å–≤–∞–¥—å–±—ã. –ú–∞—Ç—å –º–µ–Ω—è –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –Ω–µ –≥—Ä—ã–∑–ª–∞, –æ—Ç–µ—Ü –æ—Ç–¥–∞–ª —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–≤–æ–¥–æ–º. –ù–æ —ç—Ç–æ –¥–ª–∏–ª–æ—Å—å –Ω–µ–¥–æ–ª–≥–æ. –ö–æ –≤—Å–µ–º—É, –æ—Å–æ–±–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –∫ —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–µ–º—É, –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ –ø—Ä–∏–≤—ã–∫–∞–µ—à—å! –í–æ—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∫ –∂–µ–Ω–µ, –∫ —Å–≤–æ–µ–π –Ω–æ–≤–æ–π –∂–µ–Ω–µ —è –ø—Ä–∏–≤—ã–∫–Ω—É—Ç—å –Ω–µ —Å–º–æ–≥. –Ø –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–µ–≤–æ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–∏–≤–∞–ª –µ–µ —Å —Ç–æ–±–æ–π. –°—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ, —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä—è, –±—ã–ª–æ –Ω–µ –≤ –µ–µ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É. –ù–æ —á—Ç–æ-–ª–∏–±–æ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å —è
—É–∂–µ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥. –î–∞ –∏, –ø–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–¥–µ —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å, –Ω–µ —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª! –ê –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º —É –º–µ–Ω—è —Ä–æ–¥–∏–ª–∏—Å—å —Å—ã–Ω–æ–≤—å—è, –±–ª–∏–∑–Ω—è—à–∫–∏. –ö—Ä–∞—Å–∏–≤—ã–µ —Ç–∞–∫–∏–µ, —á–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–≥–ª–∞–∑—ã–µ. –ù–∞—à–∏! –ì–ª—è–¥—è –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ, –∫–∞–∫ –∂–µ–Ω–∞ –≤–æ—Ä–∫—É–µ—Ç –Ω–∞–¥ –Ω–∏–º–∏, –º–Ω–µ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏–ª–æ—Å—å –Ω–µ –ø–æ —Å–µ–±–µ, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ —è –∑–∞–º–µ—á–∞–ª, –∫–∞–∫–∏–º–∏ –≥—Ä—É—Å—Ç–Ω—ã–º–∏ –≥–ª–∞–∑–∞–º–∏ –ù–∞–¥–∏–º —Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏—Ç –Ω–∞ —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –±—Ä–∞—Ç—å–µ–≤. –ü–æ—Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ–Ω –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª –º–µ—à–∞—Ç—å. –í—Å–µ–º –º–µ—à–∞—Ç—å. –¢–æ–≥–¥–∞ —è –ø–æ–∂–∞–ª–µ–ª, —á—Ç–æ –ø–æ—à–µ–ª –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–≤–æ–¥—É —É —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π, —á—Ç–æ –∑–∞–±—Ä–∞–ª —É —Ç–µ–±—è —Å—ã–Ω–∞.
¬´–≠—Ç–∏ ¬´–∫—Ä—É—Ç—ã–µ¬ª —Å–æ–≤—Å–µ–º —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ö –ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä—è–ª–∏¬ª, ‚Äì –ø–æ–¥—É–º–∞–ª–∞ –æ–Ω–∞, –≥–ª—è–¥—è –Ω–∞
—Ç–æ, –∫–∞–∫ –∏–∑ —Ä–æ—Å–∫–æ—à–Ω–æ–≥–æ ¬´–ú–µ—Ä—Å–µ–¥–µ—Å–∞-600¬ª —Ç–æ—Ä–æ–ø–ª–∏–≤–æ –≤—ã—Å–∫–æ—á–∏–ª —ç–ª–µ–≥–∞–Ω—Ç–Ω—ã–π –º—É–∂—á–∏–Ω–∞ –ª–µ—Ç –ø—è—Ç–∏–¥–µ—Å—è—Ç–∏.
‚Äì –î–∞ –Ω–µ —Ç–æ–º–∏ —Ç—ã –µ–µ! ‚Äì –ø—Ä–∏–∫—Ä–∏–∫–Ω—É–ª–∞ –Ω–∞
–º—É–∂–∞ –ò—Ä–∏–Ω–∞ –í–∞—Å–∏–ª—å–µ–≤–Ω–∞. ‚Äì –ì–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—à—å —Ç–∞–∫, —Å–ª–æ–≤–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ –∑–∞—Å–µ–¥–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –≤—ã—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞–µ—à—å. –ö–æ—Ä–æ—á–µ!
‚Äì –¢—ã –æ–±–µ—â–∞–ª —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –º–µ–Ω—è
—Å—á–∞—Å—Ç–ª–∏–≤–æ–π! ‚Äì –≤—ã–∫—Ä–∏–∫–Ω—É–ª–∞ –ú–∞—Ä–∏–Ω–∞ –∏ –≥—Ä–æ–º–∫–æ –∑–∞—Ä—ã–¥–∞–ª–∞.
‚Äì –ê —á—Ç–æ —Ç—ã —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–ª–∞ –¥–ª—è —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —Ç–µ–±—è –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∏–ª–∏? –í–µ–¥—å —Ç—ã –Ω–∞ —Å–≤–µ—Ç –±–æ–∂–∏–π, –∫—Ä–æ–º–µ –∫–∞–∫ –≤ –æ—Ñ–∏—Å–µ –∏ –Ω–∞ –¥–∞—á–µ, –Ω–µ –ø–æ—è–≤–ª—è–µ—à—å—Å—è. –î–∞ –∏ —Ç–≤–æ—é —Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä—É –≤–æ –≤—Å–µ–π –∫—Ä–∞—Å–µ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–µ—Ä –ø–æ –∞–π–∫–∏–¥–æ –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç. –ù–æ —Ç—ã –∏ —Ç–∞–º –∑–∞–¥–Ω–∏—Ü—É —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–∑–∞–º–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—à—å! –ò–ª–∏ –¥–æ —Å–∏—Ö –ø–æ—Ä —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—à—å, —á—Ç–æ —Ç–≤–æ–π –ú—É—Ñ–∏–¥ —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –æ–ª–∏—Ü–µ—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –≤—Å–µ–π –º—É–∂—Å–∫–æ–π —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ç—ã? –ß—Ç–æ –≤—Å–µ –º—É–∂–∏–∫–∏ —Ç–∞–∫–∏–µ –∂–µ —Å–≤–æ–ª–æ—á–∏, –∫–∞–∫ –∏ –æ–Ω? –î–∞, –Ω–µ —Å–ø–æ—Ä—é, –≤ —Å–≤–æ–µ–º –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–µ –æ–Ω–∏ —Å–≤–æ–ª–æ—á–∏, –Ω–æ –Ω–µ –≤—Å–µ! –ï—Å—Ç—å –µ—â–µ –∏ –Ω–æ—Ä–º–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –º—É–∂—á–∏–Ω—ã. –í –ª—é–¥–∏ —Å–µ–±—è –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞–¥–æ! –í –ª—é–¥–∏! –ê —Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫ –Ω–µ–¥–æ–ª–≥–æ –∏ –≤ –º–æ–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—ã—Ä—å –ø–æ–ø–∞—Å—Ç—å! –¢—ã –∏ –±–µ–∑ —Ç–æ–≥–æ –≤ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–Ω–¥–∂–µ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª–∞—Å—å, —Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∏—Ç! –ü–æ–π–º–∏, —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –µ—â–µ –∏–Ω–æ–π –º–∏—Ä, –≤ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º —Ç—ã –Ω–µ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤—ã–π –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä, –Ω–æ –∏ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–Ω–∞—è, –∫—Ä–∞—Å–∏–≤–∞—è –∂–µ–Ω—â–∏–Ω–∞! –ò —ç—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–∏–Ω–µ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–∏–≤–∏–¥–µ–Ω–¥—ã –¥–∞–∂–µ –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–µ, —á–µ–º —Ç–≤–æ—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞!
–ù–∞—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–Ω–∞ –∑–Ω–∞–ª–∞, –Æ–ª—è –≤–µ–ª–∞ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–π –∏ –∑–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤—ã–π –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑ –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏, –µ–∂–µ–¥–Ω–µ–≤–Ω–æ —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–∞—è —É—Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–∏–µ –ø—Ä–æ–±–µ–∂–∫–∏ –∏ –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—è—Å—å —Ñ–∏—Ç–Ω–µ—Å–æ–º. –ò –∫ –∞–ª–∫–æ–≥–æ–ª—é, –∏ –∫ –∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω–∏—é –æ–Ω–∞
–æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏, –Ω–µ —Ä–∞–∑ —Ä—É–≥–∞—è –ú–∞—Ä–∏–Ω—É –∑–∞ —Ç–∞–π–Ω—É—é –¥—Ä—É–∂–±—É —Å –≥–æ–ª—É–±—ã–º ¬´–ü–∞—Ä–ª–∞–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–º¬ª. –°—Ç–∞–ª–æ —è—Å–Ω–æ, —á—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–æ–∏—Ç —Å–µ—Ä—å–µ–∑–Ω—ã–π.
–¶–µ–ª—É—é –Ω–æ—á—å –ú–∞—Ä–∏–Ω–∞ –Ω–µ —Å–ø–∞–ª–∞. –ï–π –Æ–ª—å–∫–∏–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –æ–º–µ—Ä–∑–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–º –∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–º. –ù–æ –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–µ —Å —Ç–µ–º —ç—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª–∞ –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ –∑–∞—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å, –∫ —Ç–æ–º—É –∂–µ, –∫–∞–∫ –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏–ª–∞ –ø–æ–¥—Ä—É–≥–∞, —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å —ç—Ç–æ –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ. –í—Å—é –Ω–æ—á—å –æ–Ω–∞ –±–æ—Ä–æ–ª–∞—Å—å —Å –º—É–∫–∞–º–∏ —Å–æ–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏. –û–Ω–∞ –Ω–µ –∑–Ω–∞–ª–∞, –∫–∞–∫ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ –ø–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∏—Ç—å. –í–µ–¥—å –µ—Å–ª–∏, –∫–∞–∫ —É—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–∞–ª–∞ –Æ–ª—è, –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —É—Å–ª—É–≥–∏ –Ω–æ—Å—è—Ç –∏—Å–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Ü–µ—Ä–µ–º–æ–Ω–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç, —Ç–æ –µ–π
—Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–µ—á–µ–≥–æ –±–æ—è—Ç—å—Å—è!
–ü—Ä–æ—à–ª–æ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª—å. –ó–∞—Ö–≤–∞—Ç—ã–≤–∞—é—â–∞—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞, –∂–∏–∑–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è —Å—É–º–∞—Ç–æ—Ö–∞ –∏ –ø–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∫–∞ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ –¥–ª—è –∞–¥–≤–æ–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Å–≥–ª–∞–¥–∏–ª–∏ –∏–∑ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∂–∏—Ç—ã–µ –æ–±–∏–¥—ã. –ë–æ–ª—å –≤–æ—Å–ø–æ–º–∏–Ω–∞–Ω–∏–π –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –æ—Ç—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞—Ç—å. –° —Ç—Ä–µ–ø–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–º –≤–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –º–æ–ª–æ–¥–∞—è –∂–µ–Ω—â–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–ª–∞ –¥–Ω–∏ –¥–æ
–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —Å—É–¥–µ–±–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–∞. –ü–æ—á—Ç–∏ –µ–∂–µ–¥–Ω–µ–≤–Ω–æ –æ–±—â–∞—è—Å—å —Å –ù–∞–¥–∏–º–æ–º –ø–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–≤–æ–º –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–µ—Ç–∞ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –°–∫–∞–π–ø, –æ–Ω–∞ —Ä–∞—Å—Å–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–ª–∞ –µ–º—É –æ —Ç–æ–º, –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–Ω—ã–µ –∏ –≤–µ—Å–µ–ª—ã–µ –±—É–¥—É—Ç —É –Ω–µ–≥–æ –¥—Ä—É–∑—å—è, –∫–∞–∫–æ–π —á—É–¥–Ω–æ–π –∏ —à–∞–ª–æ–≤–ª–∏–≤—ã–π –ø–µ—Å –æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è–µ—Ç –∏—Ö –¥–µ—Ç—Å–∫—É—é –ø–ª–æ—â–∞–¥–∫—É, –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ –¥–µ—Ä–µ–≤—å—è —Ä–∞—Å—Ç—É—Ç –ø–æ–¥ –∏—Ö –æ–∫–Ω–æ–º. –ú–∞–ª—ã—à –≤–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–ª—É—à–∞–ª –º–∞–º—É, –≥–ª—è–¥—è –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ–µ –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–º–∏ –≥—Ä—É—Å—Ç–Ω—ã–º–∏ –≥–ª–∞–∑–∞–º–∏.
‚Äì –ß—Ç–æ —Ç—ã, –º–∏–ª–∞—è, —ç—Ç–æ –∂–µ —Ç–∞–∫ –∫—Ä–∞—Å–∏–≤–æ! ‚Äì
–ø–æ—Ö–æ—Ç–ª–∏–≤–æ —É–ª—ã–±–Ω—É–ª—Å—è –ï–≤–≥–µ–Ω–∏–π –ì—Ä–∏–≥–æ—Ä—å–µ–≤–∏—á. –ò, –ø–æ—Ç—è–Ω—É–≤—à–∏—Å—å –∫ –±—É—Ç—ã–ª–∫–µ —Å –∫–æ–Ω—å—è–∫–æ–º, –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–∏–ª: ‚Äì –ú–æ–∂–µ—Ç, –∏ —Ç–µ–±–µ –Ω–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å –Ω–µ–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ?
–ü—Ä–æ—à–µ–ª —á–∞—Å. –ù–∞–∫–æ–Ω–µ—Ü –≤–æ –¥–≤–æ—Ä–µ –ø–æ—è–≤–∏–ª–∏—Å—å –ª—é–¥–∏. –í–∑–≤–æ–ª–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∏–≤–∞—è, –æ–Ω–∏
–≤–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –æ—Å–º–∞—Ç—Ä–∏–≤–∞–ª–∏ —Ç–µ—Ä—Ä–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—é. –ß–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º–∏–Ω—É—Ç –∏–∑ –¥–æ–º–∞ –≤—ã–Ω–µ—Å–ª–∏ –±–µ–∑–¥—ã—Ö–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–µ —Ç–µ–ª–æ —Ö–æ–∑—è–∏–Ω–∞, –Ω–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–æ–µ –±–µ–ª–æ–π –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—ã–Ω–µ–π. –ê–∫–∫—É—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–æ –ø–æ–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏–≤ –Ω–æ—Å–∏–ª–∫–∏ –≤ ¬´—Å–∫–æ—Ä—É—é –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å¬ª, –º–µ–¥–∏–∫–∏ —É–µ—Ö–∞–ª–∏. –ú–∏–ª–∏—Ü–∏—è –ø–æ–µ—Ö–∞–ª–∞ —Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–º.
–£—é—Ç–Ω–æ —É—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–≤—à–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞ –∑–∞–¥–Ω–µ–º —Å–∏–¥–µ–Ω—å–µ —Å–ª—É–∂–µ–±–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–æ–±–∏–ª—è, –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω –∑–∞–¥—É–º—á–∏–≤–æ —Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ–ª –≤ –æ–∫–Ω–æ.
–°–µ–≥–æ–¥–Ω—è –±—ã–ª –æ—Å–æ–±–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –¥–µ–Ω—å. –†–æ–≤–Ω–æ –ø—è—Ç–Ω–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç—å –ª–µ—Ç –Ω–∞–∑–∞–¥ —Ç—Ä–∏ –Ω–µ–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –±–µ—Å—à–∞–±–∞—à–Ω—ã—Ö –∏ –≤–µ—Å—å–º–∞ —Å–º–µ–ª—ã—Ö –ø–∞—Ä–µ–Ω—å–∫–∞, –∏–º–µ—è –≤ —Ä—É–∫–∞—Ö –¥–∏–ø–ª–æ–º—ã —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤ –∏ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–æ—â–∞–≤—à–∏—Å—å —Å–æ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å–æ–º —Å—Ç—É–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤, —Å–º–æ–≥–ª–∏ –¥–æ–≤–æ–ª—å–Ω–æ –ª–æ–≤–∫–æ –∑–∞–ø—Ä—ã–≥–Ω—É—Ç—å –Ω–∞ –∏–Ω—É—é —Å–æ—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—É—é —Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω—å, –≥–æ—Ä–¥–æ –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–≤ —Å–µ–±—è –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø—Ä–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è–º–∏. –ö–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –≤—ã–ø—É—Å–∫–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤–µ—á–µ—Ä–∞ –æ–Ω–∏ —Ä–∞–¥–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ –≤—ã–±–µ–∂–∞–ª–∏ –∑–∞ –≤–æ—Ä–æ—Ç–∞ —Ä–æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ–ª–∏—Ç–µ—Ö–∞, –∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ—Å—å, —á—Ç–æ –≤–µ—Å—å –º–∏—Ä –ª–µ–∂–∏—Ç —É –∏—Ö –Ω–æ–≥. –ò –æ–Ω–∏ —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª–∏ –µ–≥–æ –≤–∑—è—Ç—å ‚Äì –≤–µ—Å—å –∏ —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É. –î—É–º–∞–µ—Ç–µ, –Ω–µ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏–ª–æ—Å—å? –û—à–∏–±–∞–µ—Ç–µ—Å—å! –ì–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ–µ ‚Äì –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—é. –ê —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–¥–Ω–∞: –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–∞—è. –ö–∞–∫ –∂–µ –∏–Ω–∞—á–µ, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –∫—Ä–æ–≤—å –∫–∏–ø–∏—Ç, –∑–∞ –ø–ª–µ—á–∞–º–∏ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ –¥–≤–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç—å –¥–≤–∞, –∞ –≤–ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∏ —Å—Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏ –Ω–µ–∏–∑–≤–µ–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ!
–ê —Ç–∞–∫ –∫–∞–∫ –≤—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞—Ç—å –≤ —Å—Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∫—É —Å —ç—Ç–∏–º –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω—ã–º –∏ —Å–∏–ª—å–Ω—ã–º –º–∏—Ä–æ–º –±–µ–∑ –æ—Å–æ–±–æ–π –ø–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∫–∏ –±—ã–ª–æ —Ä–∏—Å–∫–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ, —Å–≤–æ—é —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫—É –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª–∏ –Ω–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞–¥–µ–∂–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏ –¥–æ–≤–æ–ª—å–Ω–æ –∫—Ä–µ–ø–∫–æ–≥–æ —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ —Ç—ã–ª–∞.
–° –≥—Ä—É—Å—Ç—å—é –≤–∑–¥–æ—Ö–Ω—É–≤, –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–π –ø–æ–≥—Ä—É–∑–∏–ª—Å—è –≤ –≤–æ—Å–ø–æ–º–∏–Ω–∞–Ω–∏—è.
–®–ª–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–µ –≥–æ–¥—ã –ø–æ—Å—Ç—Å–æ–≤–µ—Ç—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ ¬´—Ä–∞–∑–±—Ä–æ–¥–∞ –∏ —à–∞—Ç–∞–Ω–∏—è¬ª. –ö—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–¥–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ –±–µ–≥–∞–ª —Å —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏ –ø–æ –ø–ª–æ—â–∞–¥—è–º —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏—Ö –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–æ–≤, —Ä–∞–¥—É—è—Å—å —Ç–∞–∫ –Ω–µ–æ–∂–∏–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏—à–µ–¥—à–µ–π –Ω–µ–∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏. –ö—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ, –ø–æ–¥–ø–µ—Ä–µ–≤ —Å—Ç–µ–Ω—ã –ø—É—Å—Ç—ã—Ö –≥–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–Ω–æ–º–æ–≤, —Ç–æ–º–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∞–∏–≤–∞–ª –≤ –æ—á–µ—Ä–µ–¥—è—Ö –∑–∞ –≤–æ–∂–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –∫—É—Å–∫–æ–º –º–∞—Å–ª–∞ –∏ –±–ª–µ–¥–Ω—ã–º–∏ –æ—Ç –æ–±–∏–ª–∏—è —Å–æ–∏ ¬´–®–∫–æ–ª—å–Ω—ã–º–∏¬ª —Å–æ—Å–∏—Å–∫–∞–º–∏. –ê –∫—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ, –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ —Å–æ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–∏–≤, —á—Ç–æ –∫ —á–µ–º—É, –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª: –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ—Ç –ö–ü–°–°, —Ç–æ –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –∂–µ –∫—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–æ–º. –û—Å–æ–±–æ –Ω–µ –∂–∞–¥–Ω–∏—á–∞—è, –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏–≤ –¥–µ–º–æ–∫—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—é –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–æ–≤, –∏–∑ –∫—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∏–≤—ã—Ö ¬´–Ω–∞–ø–µ—Ä—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤¬ª –∏ ¬´–∫–∏–¥–∞–ª¬ª –æ–Ω–∏ –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∫–≤–∞–ª–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –≤ –¥–∏—Å—Ü–∏–ø–ª–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ ¬´–±—Ä–∏–≥–∞–¥—ã¬ª, –≤–∑—è–≤ –ø–æ–¥ —Å–≤–æ–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–ª—å –≤—Å–µ, —á—Ç–æ –±—Ä–∞–ª–æ—Å—å, –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞—è —Å –ø—Ä–∏–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–æ—Ä–æ–≥ –∏ –∑–∞–∫–∞–Ω—á–∏–≤–∞—è —Ç–æ—Ä–≥–æ–≤—ã–º–∏ —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–º–∏ –∏ –∫–∞–∑–∏–Ω–æ. –í—Å–µ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –∏ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –Ω–∞—Ä–∞—â–∏–≤–∞—è —Å–≤–æ–µ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤–æ–µ –º–æ–≥—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ, –æ–Ω–∏ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏–ª–∏ —Å–µ–±—è –∫ —Å–≤–µ—Ç–ª–æ–º—É –±—É–¥—É—â–µ–º—É –Ω–æ–≤–æ—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–ª–∏–≥–∞—Ä—Ö–æ–≤.
–ù–æ —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å—Å—è —Å–∞–º–∏ —Å —Ç–∞–∫–∏–º –ø—ã—à–Ω—ã–º, —Ö–æ—Ç—è –∏ –±–µ—Å—Ö–æ–∑–Ω—ã–º –ø–∏—Ä–æ–≥–æ–º —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∞–ª–∏–≤–∞—é—â–µ–π—Å—è —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∏ –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥–ª–∏. –ò —Ç—É—Ç, –æ–∫–æ–Ω—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –ø–æ–Ω—è–≤, —á—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ—à–ª–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –≤–µ—Ä–Ω—É—Ç—å, –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ –ø—Ä–∏—à–ª–∏ –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å –±—ã–≤—à–∏–µ –Ω–æ–º–µ–Ω–∫–ª–∞—Ç—É—Ä—â–∏–∫–∏. –°–ø—Ä—è—Ç–∞–≤ –Ω–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–∏–π —Å–ª—É—á–∞–π —Å–≤–æ–∏ –ø–∞—Ä—Ç–±–∏–ª–µ—Ç—ã –∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–æ–¥–µ–≤—à–∏—Å—å –≤ –≤—ã—à–∏—Ç—ã–µ —Å–æ—Ä–æ—á–∫–∏, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è –µ—â–µ –≤–µ—Å—å–º–∞ —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ —Ä—ã—á–∞–≥–∏ –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏, –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∏ —Å—Ç—Ä–µ–º–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å ¬´–ø—Ä–∏—Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏¬ª.
–ù–µ –æ–±–æ—à–ª–∏ —ç—Ç–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω—ã –∏ –∏—Ö —Å–µ–º—å—é. –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω-—Å—Ç–∞—Ä—à–∏–π, –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞–≤—à–∏–π —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞ –¥–æ–≤–æ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–æ–ª–∏–¥–Ω—É—é –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–π –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ —Å—Ç–æ–ª–∏—Ü—ã, –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∞–ª–∞ –°–æ—é–∑–∞ —Ç–æ–∂–µ –∑–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–≤–Ω–∏—á–∞–ª, —Å –Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª—å–∫—É —É–≥—Ä—é–º–æ –ø–æ–º–æ–ª—á–∞–ª, –∞ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –Ω–µ–æ–∂–∏–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ –±–æ–¥—Ä–æ –∑–∞—è–≤–∏–ª:
‚Äì –ù—É –∏ —Å–ª–∞–≤–∞ –±–æ–≥—É, —á—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫ –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–æ—à–ª–æ! –ì–ö–ß–ü –Ω–∞–º –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–º —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–æ–º–æ–≥. –ì–Ω–∏–ª–∞—è –±—ã–ª–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞, –ø–æ–ø—É–ª–∏—Å—Ç—Å–∫–∞—è! –û–Ω–∞ —Å —Å–µ–º–Ω–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç–æ–≥–æ –≥–æ–¥–∞ –±—ã–ª–∞ –æ–±—Ä–µ—á–µ–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª. –≠–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∞ –Ω–∞—à–∞ –ª–∏—à—å –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ—Ñ—Ç–µ–¥–æ–ª–ª–∞—Ä–µ –∏ –¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞–ª–∞—Å—å. –Ø –¥–∞–≤–Ω–æ —É–∂–µ –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª, —á—Ç–æ –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∏–∑–º –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã–ª–æ –ø–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –≤–∑—è—Ç–æ–π –¢—é–º–µ–Ω—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏. –í–µ–¥—å —É –Ω–∞—Å —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–ª–æ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª–æ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–æ —Å ¬´–æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–∫–æ–π¬ª. –ê –Ω–∞—Ä–æ–¥ –∫–æ–∫—Å–æ–º –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–∫–æ—Ä–º–∏—à—å –¥–∞ —Ç—Ä—É–±—ã –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–æ —à—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–¥–µ–Ω–µ—à—å! –î–≤–∏–≥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è–º–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–µ—Å—Å–∞ —è–≤–ª—è—é—Ç—Å—è —á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∞—è —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∏ –∑–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤–∞—è –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ü–∏—è. –í–æ—Ç —á—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–º –Ω–∞–¥–æ!
–ù–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–∑–∞–¥–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ, –º–∞–º–∞ —Å –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–µ–º —É–¥–∏–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–∞–±–ª—é–¥–∞–ª–∏, –∫–∞–∫, –±–æ–¥—Ä–æ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–≤ –ø–ª–µ—á–∏, –Ω–µ–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∏—Å—Ç, –Ω–µ —É–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–≤—à–∏–π —Å–ª—É—á–∞—è –ø—Ä–∏ —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–∏—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤–µ–ª–∏–∫–æ–≥–æ –ú–∞—Ä–∫—Å–∞, —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏–≤–∞–ª –Ω–æ–≤—É—é —Ç–µ–æ—Ä–∏—é —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–≤–µ—Ç–∞–Ω–∏—è —Å–≤–æ–µ–π —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—ã. –ë—É–¥—É—á–∏ —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞ —é–Ω—ã–º —Å—Ç—É–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–º, –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–ª —Å–≤–æ–µ–º—É —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—é –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ, —á–µ–º –ª—é–±–æ–º—É –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∏–∫—É –º–∞—Ä–∫—Å–∏–∑–º–∞-–ª–µ–Ω–∏–Ω–∏–∑–º–∞. –° –≤–æ—Å—Ö–∏—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º —Å–ª—É—à–∞—è –µ–≥–æ –≥—Ä–∞–Ω–¥–∏–æ–∑–Ω—ã–µ –ø–ª–∞–Ω—ã, –æ–Ω –∏—Å–∫—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–µ –≤–µ—Ä–∏–ª —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º –æ—Ç—Ü–∞.
–û–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª—å –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω-—Å—Ç–∞—Ä—à–∏–π —É—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–ª—Å—è –Ω–∞ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –∑–∞–≤–æ–¥–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–æ–≤, –∞ –º–∞—Ç—É—à–∫–∞ –∏–∑ –≤–µ–¥—É—â–µ–≥–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –≤ –∑–∞–≤–µ–¥—É—é—â—É—é –ø–æ–ª—É—Ä–∞–∑–≤–∞–ª–∏–≤—à–µ–π—Å—è —Ç–∞—Ä–Ω–æ–π –±–∞–∑–æ–π, –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–π –±—ã–ª –¥–∞–ª–µ–∫–æ –Ω–µ –≤ –≤–æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–≥–µ.
‚Äì –ù–µ –∑–Ω–∞–µ—à—å –µ—â–µ —Ç—ã –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏, —Å—Ç—É–¥–µ–Ω—Ç! ‚Äì –æ–±–∏–∂–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —É—Ö–º—ã–ª—å–Ω—É–ª—Å—è –æ—Ç–µ—Ü. ‚Äì –ò –º–æ–π –∑–∞–≤–æ–¥, –∏ –º–∞–º–∏–Ω–∞ –±–∞–∑–∞ –ø–æ–∫–∞ —á—Ç–æ —è–≤–ª—è—é—Ç—Å—è –≥–æ—Å—É–¥–∞—Ä—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∏—è–º–∏. –ü–æ–¥—á–µ—Ä–∫–∏–≤–∞—é: –ø–æ–∫–∞! –£–∂–µ –ø–æ –≤—Å–µ–π —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å –ø—Ä–∏–≤–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏. –ê –∫—Ç–æ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –∏–º–µ–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∏–π? –û—Ç–≤–µ—á–∞—é: –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤! –ê –∫—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–æ–∏—Ç –≤–æ –≥–ª–∞–≤–µ –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–∞? –î–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä! –°–µ—á–µ—à—å, —Å—ã–Ω–æ–∫? –ü—É—Å—Ç—å —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –º–æ–π –∑–∞–≤–æ–¥ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–ª–Ω—É—é –º–æ—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–∞—Ä–æ–¥ –≤ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –±–µ–¥–Ω—ã–π, –µ–º—É —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –Ω–µ –¥–æ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–∞. –ù–æ –ø—Ä–∏–¥—É—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∞, ‚Äì –∞ –æ–Ω–∏, –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å, –Ω–µ –∑–∞ –≥–æ—Ä–∞–º–∏. –¢–æ–≥–¥–∞ –∏ –ø–æ–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏–º! –ò –º–∞—Ç—å —Ç–≤–æ—é —è –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–µ –æ–±–∏–¥–µ–ª. –ù—É —Å–∏–¥–µ–ª–∞ –æ–Ω–∞, –∫–æ—Ä–ø–µ–ª–∞ –Ω–∞–¥ —Å–≤–æ–∏–º–∏ —á–µ—Ä—Ç–µ–∂–∞–º–∏. –ê –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤, –µ—Å–ª–∏ —Ç—ã –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–ª –≤–Ω–∏–º–∞–Ω–∏–µ, –≤—Å–µ –º–µ–Ω—å—à–µ –∏ –º–µ–Ω—å—à–µ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—Å—è. –í–µ–¥—å –∏—Ö –ö–ë –Ω–∞ –ú–æ—Å–∫–≤—É —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç. –¢—ã –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—à—å, –æ —á–µ–º —è? –î–æ–ª–≥–æ –ª–∏ –µ—â–µ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –±—Ä–∞–∫–æ—Ä–∞–∑–≤–æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–∞ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–¥–æ–ª–∂–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –∏—Ö —Å–æ—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ? –ù–µ –¥—É–º–∞—é! –ê —è —Ç–≤–æ—é –º–∞—Ç—å –∫–µ–º –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏–ª? –ó–∞–≤–µ–¥—É—é—â–µ–π! –ù—É –∏ –ø—É—Å—Ç—å —É –Ω–µ–µ –≤ –ø–æ–¥—á–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ –¥–≤–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç—å —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫. –ù—É –∏ –ø—É—Å—Ç—å –≤—Å–µ —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥—ã –Ω–∞ –µ–µ –±–∞–∑–µ –¥–∞–≤–Ω–æ —Å–≥–Ω–∏–ª–∏. –ó–∞—Ç–æ –±–∞–∑–∞ —ç—Ç–∞ –≤ –ü—É—â–µ-–í–æ–¥–∏—Ü–µ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è. –°–∏–¥–∏—Ç —Ç–≤–æ—è –º–∞—Ç—É—à–∫–∞ –≤ —Å–æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–æ–º –±–æ—Ä—É, –∫–∞–∫ —Ü–∞—Ä–∏—Ü–∞, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –∑–µ–º–ª—è —Ç–∞–º –±–µ—Å—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è!
–ó–Ω–∞–ª –ª–∏ –æ–Ω —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞, —á—Ç–æ —ç—Ç–∏ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω—É—Ç –ø—Ä–æ—Ä–æ—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º–∏? –í—Å–µ–≥–æ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ª–µ—Ç –æ—Ç–µ—Ü —Å—Ç–∞–ª –≤–ª–∞–¥–µ–ª—å—Ü–µ–º –¥–µ–≤—è–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ –∞–∫—Ü–∏–π —Å–≤–æ–µ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∏—è, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–µ –∫ —Ç–æ–º—É –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ
–ø–æ—Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–∞–±–∏—Ä–∞—Ç—å –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ—Ç—ã. –¢–∞—Ä–Ω–∞—è –±–∞–∑–∞, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–π —Ä—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–¥–∏–ª–∞ –º–∞—Ç—å, –∑–∞ —ç—Ç–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é –ø—Ä–µ–∫—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–ª–∞ —Å–≤–æ—é –¥–µ—è—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å. –û—Ç –±–µ–∑—ã—Å—Ö–æ–¥–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏, –ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–≤ –∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ —Ä—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—é, —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–∏ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∏ –ª—É—á—à–µ–π –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏. –ò –ø–æ–∫–∞ –∞—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä—ã —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–ª–∏ –Ω–∞–¥ –≤–ø–µ—á–∞—Ç–ª—è—é—â–∏–º –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–æ–º –≥–æ—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∏—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–º–ø–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞, —Ç–µ—Ä—Ä–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è –±–∞–∑—ã –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–µ –¥–∏–≤–∏–¥–µ–Ω–¥—ã.
–¢–∞–∫ –∏ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª—Å—è –∏—Ö –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Å–µ–º–µ–π–Ω—ã–π –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å.
–ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞, –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∏–≤—à–∏—Å—å, –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–π –∑–∞—è–≤–∏–ª –æ —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –Ω–∞–ø–æ–ª–µ–æ–Ω–æ–≤—Å–∫–∏—Ö –ø–ª–∞–Ω–∞—Ö, —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏ –Ω–µ —Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏ —Ä–∞–∑–¥—É–º—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–∏–ª–∏—Å—å. –ù–æ —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–µ–æ–∂–∏–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–æ–≤–æ–∏—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–º—É –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å–º–µ–Ω—É –±—ã–ª–æ –≤—ã–¥–≤–∏–Ω—É—Ç–æ –∫–∞—Ç–µ–≥–æ—Ä–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ: –ø–æ–∫–∞ –Ω–µ –∂–µ–Ω–∏—à—å—Å—è, –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å –Ω–µ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—à—å.
‚Äì –ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ç—ã —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—à—å —Å–µ–±—è –¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ –≤–∑—Ä–æ—Å–ª—ã–º –¥–ª—è —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –Ω–∞—á–∞—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–µ –¥–µ–ª–æ, –ø–æ—á–µ–º—É –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º —É—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–∞–µ—à—å, —á—Ç–æ –º–æ–ª–æ–¥ –¥–ª—è —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è —Å–µ–º—å–∏? –û–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Å—å, —Å—ã–Ω–æ–∫! ‚Äì –≤—Å–∫–∏–ø–µ–ª –æ—Ç–µ—Ü. ‚Äì –¢–µ–±–µ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∞–±–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, –∞ –Ω–µ —Ä–æ–π –∑–ª–∞—Ç–æ–∫—É–¥—Ä—ã—Ö –Ω–∏–º—Ñ! –í–µ–¥—å —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å —Å—Ç—É–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ—Ç–ª–∏—á–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –æ—Ç —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å–∞ –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å–º–µ–Ω–∞. –¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –∏ –¥–µ–≤—á–æ–Ω–∫–∏ –Ω–∞ —Ç–µ–±—è –ø–æ-–¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–º—É —Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å –±—É–¥—É—Ç. –û–Ω–∏ –≤ —Ç–≤–æ–∏—Ö –≥–ª–∞–∑–∞—Ö –Ω–µ –ª—é–±–æ–≤—å –±—É–¥—É—Ç –∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å, –∞ –∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ –æ—Ç—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–æ–ª–ª–∞—Ä–∞! –ó–∞–ø–æ–º–Ω–∏: –¥–µ–Ω—å–≥–∏ –¥–ª—è –∂–µ–Ω—â–∏–Ω ‚Äì —ç—Ç–æ –∫–∞–∫ ¬´–í–∏–∞–≥—Ä–∞¬ª –¥–ª—è –º—É–∂—á–∏–Ω!
–û—Ç—á–∞—è–Ω–Ω–æ —Å–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤–ª—è—è—Å—å, –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–Ω–µ–π –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ–ª –≤ –≥–ª—É–±–æ–∫–∏—Ö —Ä–∞–∑–¥—É–º—å—è—Ö. –ê –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º —Ä–µ—à–∏–ª, —á—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫ –æ–Ω–æ, –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç, –∏ –∫ –ª—É—á—à–µ–º—É. –ü–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–∞–≤ –≤ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–µ –∫–∞–Ω–¥–∏–¥–∞—Ç—É—Ä—ã –ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –Ω–µ–≤–µ—Å—Ç, –æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏–ª —Å–≤–æ–π –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ —Å–æ–∫—É—Ä—Å–Ω–∏—Ü–µ, —Å–∫—Ä–æ–º–Ω–æ–π –∏ –º–∏–ª–æ–≤–∏–¥–Ω–æ–π –ù–∞—Ç–∞—à–∫–µ –†–æ—â–∏–Ω–æ–π. –£ –Ω–∏—Ö –≤—Ä–æ–¥–µ –∏ –ª—é–±–≤–∏ –æ—Å–æ–±–æ–π –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–æ ‚Äì —Ç–∞–∫, –≤—Å—Ç—Ä–µ—á–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –∏–Ω–æ–≥–¥–∞. –í—Ä–µ–º—è –æ—Ç –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≤ –µ–µ –∫–æ–º–Ω–∞—Ç–µ –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–æ –ø–æ–¥—Ä—É–≥ –ø–æ –æ–±—â–µ–∂–∏—Ç–∏—é, –æ–Ω —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–æ —Ü–µ–ª–æ–≤–∞–ª –µ–µ –≥–æ—Ä—è—á–∏–µ, —Å–ª–∞–¥–∫–∏–µ –≥—É–±—ã. –ê –æ–Ω–∞ –ø–æ—á–µ–º—É-—Ç–æ –≤–∑–¥—ã—Ö–∞–ª–∞, –ø—Ä–æ–≤–æ–∂–∞—è –µ–≥–æ –∫ –¥–≤–µ—Ä–∏.
–í–∑–≤–µ—Å–∏–≤ —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ –≤—Å–µ ¬´–∑–∞¬ª –∏ ¬´–ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤¬ª –∏ –¥–∞–∂–µ –Ω–µ–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–±—Ä–∞–¥–æ–≤–∞–≤—à–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞–º–µ—á–∞—é—â–∏–º—Å—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∞–º, –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω, –Ω–µ –º–µ—à–∫–∞—è, –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—Å—è –≤ –û–¥–µ—Å—Å—É. –ò —É–∂–µ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª—é –≤–µ—Ä–Ω—É–ª—Å—è –¥–æ–º–æ–π —Å–æ —Å—á–∞—Å—Ç–ª–∏–≤–æ–π –Ω–µ–≤–µ—Å—Ç–æ–π –∏ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞—é—â–∏–º–∏—Å—è –ø–µ—Ä—Å–ø–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–∞–º–∏. –†–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏, –≤–∏–¥—è —Å–µ—Ä—å–µ–∑–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ –Ω–∞–º–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–π, –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∏ –ø–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∫—É –∫ —Å–≤–∞–¥—å–±–µ. –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–π –∂–µ, –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è–≤ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª–∞ –∏–≥—Ä—ã, –æ–±–ª–∞—á–∏–ª—Å—è –≤ –¥–æ—Ä–æ–≥–æ–π –∫–æ—Å—Ç—é–º –∏, —Å–∏—è—è –Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω—å–∫–∏–º –ø–æ—Ä—Ç—Ñ–µ–ª–µ–º –∏–∑ –∫—Ä–æ–∫–æ–¥–∏–ª—å–µ–π –∫–æ–∂–∏, –∑–∞–Ω—è–ª—Å—è –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–∏–µ–º —Ñ–∏—Ä–º—ã. –ù–æ —Ä–µ–¥–∫–æ –≤ –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏ –±—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç –≤—Å–µ –≥–ª–∞–¥–∫–æ. –ò–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –≤ —Ç–æ—Ç –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞, –∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –±—ã, –≤—Å–µ —Ç–∞–∫ –∑–∞–º–µ—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —É—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–ª–æ—Å—å, –≤–æ–∑–Ω–∏–∫–ª–∏ –Ω–æ–≤—ã–µ —Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏. –ì–æ—Ä–æ–¥—Å–∫–∏–µ –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–µ –¥–∞–≤–∞–ª–∏ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ –≥–æ—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∏—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–º–ø–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞ –≤ –ü—É—â–µ-–í–æ–¥–∏—Ü–µ. –î–æ–ª–≥–æ –æ–±–∏–≤–∞—è –ø–æ—Ä–æ–≥–∏ —Å—Ç–æ–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã—Ö –∫–∞–±–∏–Ω–µ—Ç–æ–≤, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è —Å—Ç–∞—Ä—ã–µ –æ—Ç—Ü–æ–≤—Å–∫–∏–µ —Å–≤—è–∑–∏, –æ–Ω –≤—Å–µ —Ä–∞–≤–Ω–æ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥ —Ä–µ—à–∏—Ç—å —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å. –í–µ–¥—å –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å –≤ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ –æ–±—Ä–µ–ª–∞ —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –∏–Ω–æ–µ –ª–∏—Ü–æ.
–ò —Ç—É—Ç –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å –ø—Ä–∏—à–µ–ª –¥–æ–±—Ä—ã–π –ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–µ–ª—å –∏ —Å–æ–∫—É—Ä—Å–Ω–∏–∫ –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ—è, –î–∏–º–∞ –ö–æ—Ä–Ω–∏–µ–Ω–∫–æ. –í —Ç–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –µ–≥–æ –æ—Ç–µ—Ü –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–∏–π –ø–æ—Å—Ç –≤ –¥–µ–ø–∞—Ä—Ç–∞–º–µ–Ω—Ç–µ –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ö–æ–∑—è–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –ö–∏–µ–≤–∞. –ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É –ö–æ—Ä–Ω–∏–µ–Ω–∫–æ –º–æ–≥ —Ä–µ—à–∏—Ç—å –ª—é–±—É—é –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—É. –û—Å–æ–±–æ –Ω–µ —Å—Ç–µ—Å–Ω—è—è—Å—å, –æ–Ω –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–∏–ª —Å–≤–æ–∏ —É—Å–ª—É–≥–∏ –∏ –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å –≤ –æ–±–º–µ–Ω –Ω–∞ –¥–æ–ª–µ–≤–æ–µ —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–µ —Å—ã–Ω–∞ –≤ –±—É–¥—É—â–µ–π —Ñ–∏—Ä–º–µ. –ü–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞—è –≤—ã–≥–æ–¥—É –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç–∞, –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–∏–ª—Å—è. –ù–æ –∏ –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–µ —Å–º–æ–≥–ª–∏ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Ç–æ—á–∫—É. –ö–∞–∫ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–Ω–∏ —Å –ö–æ—Ä–Ω–µ–µ–º, –∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–ª–∏ —Ç–æ–≥–æ –≤ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—É—Ç–µ, —É—Å–µ–ª–∏—Å—å –∑–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—á–∏–µ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç—ã —Ñ–∏—Ä–º—ã, —Ç–æ –Ω–µ–æ–∂–∏–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª–∏, —á—Ç–æ –∏—Ö –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–µ —Å–æ–≤—Å–µ–º —Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞—é—Ç —Å –≤–æ–∑–Ω–∏–∫—à–∏–º–∏ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤—ã–º–∏ –ø–æ—Ç—Ä–µ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—è–º–∏. –†–µ–±—è—Ç–∞–º –∫–∞—Ç–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –Ω–µ —Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∞–ª–æ —Å—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–≤.
–ò–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ –≤—ã–ø—É—Å–∫–Ω–æ–º –≤–µ—á–µ—Ä–µ, —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∏–≤–∞—è –æ —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞—Ö —Å –¥—Ä—É–∑—å—è–º–∏, –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–µ–æ–∂–∏–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–∞—à–ª–∏ —Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å–µ–≥–æ –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω—å–æ–Ω–∞.
–í–∞–ª–µ—Ä–∫–∞ –ï—Ä–º–∞–∫–æ–≤ –±—ã–ª –≤–µ—Å—å–º–∞ —à—É—Å—Ç—Ä—ã–º –∏ —Ç–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤—ã–º –ø–∞—Ä–Ω–µ–º. –ü—Ä–∏–¥—è –≤ –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø—É –Ω–∞ —Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å–µ–º –∫—É—Ä—Å–µ, –æ–Ω –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ —Å—Ç–∞–ª –¥—É—à–æ–π –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–∞, –±–µ–∑ –Ω–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª–æ—Å—å –Ω–∏ –æ–¥–Ω–æ —Å–µ—Ä—å–µ–∑–Ω–æ–µ –º–µ—Ä–æ–ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∏–µ. –ë—É–¥—É—á–∏ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä—à–µ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–∫—É—Ä—Å–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤ –Ω–∞ –¥–≤–∞ –≥–æ–¥–∞, –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ–Ω —Å—Ç–∞–ª –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä–æ–º –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø—ã, —Å –º–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≥–æ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –≤—Å–µ ‚Äì –∏ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∞, –∏ –ø—Ä–µ–ø–æ–¥–∞–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–∏. –í —ç—Ç–æ–º –Ω–µ–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –±–µ—Å—à–∞–±–∞—à–Ω–æ–º –ø–∞—Ä–Ω–µ –ª—é–¥–µ–π –ø—Ä–∏—Ç—è–≥–∏–≤–∞–ª–∞ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–æ—Å—Ç—å –¥—É—à–∏ –∏ –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω–æ–µ –æ–±–∞—è–Ω–∏–µ. –û–Ω –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –∫–∏—á–∏–ª—Å—è —Å–≤–æ–∏–º –∞—Ä–º–µ–π—Å–∫–∏–º –ø—Ä–æ—à–ª—ã–º, –≤ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º –ª–∏—Ü–æ–º –∫ –ª–∏—Ü—É —Å—Ç–∞–ª–∫–∏–≤–∞–ª—Å—è —Å –∫—Ä–æ–≤—å—é –∏ —Å–º–µ—Ä—Ç—å—é. –ï—Ä–º–∞–∫–æ–≤ —Ü–µ–Ω–∏–ª –∂–∏–∑–Ω—å –∏ –∏—Å–∫—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—é—é –º—É–∂—Å–∫—É—é –¥—Ä—É–∂–±—É. –ò–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Ç–∞–º, –≤ –ß–µ—á–Ω–µ, –æ–Ω —É–∑–Ω–∞–ª, –≤ —á–µ–º –Ω–∞—Å—Ç–æ—è—â–∏–π —Å–º—ã—Å–ª –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏.
–ü–æ—Å–ª—É—à–∞–≤ —Ä–∞—Å—Å—É–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥—Ä—É–∑–µ–π, –í–∞–ª–µ—Ä–∫–∞ —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª, —á—Ç–æ —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–µ –≥–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –∂–µ–ª–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º –∏–¥—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—É—é –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –æ–∫–æ–Ω—á–∞–Ω–∏—è –ö–ü–ò —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É —Å–æ —Å–∫—É—á–Ω—ã–º —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º–æ–º –∏ –Ω–µ–æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –ø–µ—Ä—Å–ø–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–æ–π. –û–Ω —Ç–æ–∂–µ –º–µ—á—Ç–∞–ª –æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–∏ —Ñ–∏—Ä–º—ã, –Ω–æ –≤ –æ–¥–∏–Ω–æ—á–∫—É –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞—Ç—å —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å –ø–æ–∫–∞ –Ω–µ —Ä–µ—à–∞–ª—Å—è. –ï—Ä–º–∞–∫–æ–≤ –∑–∞–º–µ—Ç–∏–ª, —á—Ç–æ –µ–≥–æ —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏, –¥–æ–ª–≥–æ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–≤—à–∏–µ –≤ —Ç–æ—Ä–≥–æ–≤–ª–µ, –∞ —Ç–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä–∏–≤—à–∏–µ –Ω–∞ —Å–µ–±—è –Ω–æ–≤—É—é —Ä–æ–ª—å ¬´—á–µ–ª–Ω–æ–∫–æ–≤¬ª, –≤–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ –º–æ–≥—É—Ç –ø–æ–º–æ—á—å –∑–∞–ª–∞—Ç–∞—Ç—å –∏—Ö —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤—ã–µ –¥—ã—Ä—ã. –ú–Ω–æ–≥–æ–µ –æ–±—Å—É–¥–∏–≤, –æ–Ω–∏ —É–¥–∞—Ä–∏–ª–∏ –ø–æ —Ä—É–∫–∞–º –∏ –ø–æ–æ–±–µ—â–∞–ª–∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥ –¥—Ä—É–≥—É —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ–µ –ø–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–µ—Ä—Å—Ç–≤–æ –∏ –≤–∑–∞–∏–º–æ–≤—ã—Ä—É—á–∫—É.
–¢–∞–∫ –∏ —Ä–æ–¥–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –∏—Ö –ø–µ—Ä–≤–∞—è –∫–æ–º–º–µ—Ä—á–µ—Å–∫–∞—è —Ñ–∏—Ä–º–∞, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è –∏–∑ —Å–∫—Ä–æ–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–±—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ —Å –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é –ø–æ—Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ä–æ—Å–ª–∞ –≤ —Å–æ–ª–∏–¥–Ω—É—é —Ö–æ–ª–¥–∏–Ω–≥–æ–≤—É—é –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏—é, –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—é—â—É—é—Å—è —Ç–æ—Ä–≥–æ–≤–ª–µ–π –∏ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ–º –∂–∏–ª—å—è, –≥–æ—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∏—á–Ω—ã–º –∏ —Ç—É—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å–æ–º, –≤–ª–∞–¥–µ—é—â—É—é —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Ç–æ—Ä–≥–æ–≤–æ–π –∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º—ã—à–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Å–µ—Ç—å—é. –ò –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–∏ –Ω–∞—Ä–∞—â–∏–≤–∞–ª–∏ —Å–≤–æ–µ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤–æ–µ –º–æ–≥—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ, –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã —Å—Ç—Ä–µ–º–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –Ω–∏ –º–µ–Ω—è–ª–∏ —Å–≤–æ–π —Å–æ—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å, ‚Äì –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –æ—Ç–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –æ—Ç —Ç–µ—Å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏ –Ω–∞–¥–µ–∂–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–æ—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Å–æ–±–æ–π.
–°–ª–µ–¥—É—è —á–µ—Ç–∫–æ–º—É —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é –æ–±—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–µ–π, –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–π –∏–∑ –Ω–∏—Ö –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª—Å—è —Å–≤–æ–∏–º –¥–µ–ª–æ–º. –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω –∫—É—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ, –ö–æ—Ä–Ω–∏–µ–Ω–∫–æ —Ä—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–¥–∏–ª —Ç—É—Ä–∏–∑–º–æ–º –∏ –≥–æ—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∏—á–Ω—ã–º –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å–æ–º, –∞ –ï—Ä–º–∞–∫–æ–≤ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏–≤–∞–ª –ø–∞—Ç—Ä–æ–Ω–∞–∂ –Ω–∞–¥ —Ç–æ—Ä–≥–æ–≤–ª–µ–π. –£—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞—è –∂–∏–∑–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –æ–ø—ã—Ç –í–∞–ª–µ—Ä–∫–∏, –µ–≥–æ –º—É–¥—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—å –∏ –ø—Ä–∞–≥–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–º, –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –µ–≥–æ –∏–∑–±—Ä–∞–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å–µ–¥–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–º –ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏—Ö –∞–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–±—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞, —Å–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–µ–º –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ä–æ—Å—à–µ–≥–æ –≤ –¥–æ–≤–æ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–æ–ª–∏–¥–Ω–æ–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∏–µ —Å –ø–æ–º–ø–µ–∑–Ω—ã–º –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º ¬´—Ö–æ–ª–¥–∏–Ω–≥–æ–≤–∞—è –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏—è¬ª.
–ó–∞ —ç—Ç–∏ –ø—è—Ç–Ω–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç—å –ª–µ—Ç –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–æ—Å—å. –ò–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–∏—Å—å –∏ –æ–Ω–∏, –∏—Ö —Ö–∞—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–µ—Ä—ã –∏ –¥–∞–∂–µ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø—ã. –ö—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–∞–ª —á—É—Ç–æ—á–∫—É –ª–µ–Ω–∏–≤–µ–µ –∏ –≤–∞–ª—å—è–∂–Ω–µ–µ, –∫—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ ‚Äì –∞–∑–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–µ–µ –∏ –±–µ—Å—à–∞–±–∞—à–Ω–µ–µ, –∫—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–ª—Å—è —Å–µ—Ä—å–µ–∑–Ω–µ–µ –∏ –∑–ª–µ–µ, –Ω–æ –≤—Å–µ —Ä–∞–≤–Ω–æ –æ–Ω–∏ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ–π.

–ê –≤–µ–¥—å –Ω–µ–¥–∞–≤–Ω–æ –≤—Å–µ –±—ã–ª–æ –ø–æ-–¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–º—É. –ë—ã–ª–∞ —Å–µ–º—å—è, –±—ã–ª–∞ –ª—é–±–æ–≤—å. –ë—ã–ª–∏ –∂–µ–Ω–∞ –∏ –¥–æ—á—å. –î–∞–∂–µ –∫–æ—à–∫–∞ –±—ã–ª–∞. –ê –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç, –µ–º—É —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ—Å—å, —á—Ç–æ –≤—Å–µ —ç—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª–æ. –ë—ã–ª–æ‚Ä¶ –±—ã–ª–æ‚Ä¶ –±—ã–ª–æ‚Ä¶
–í —Ç–æ—Ç –¥–µ–Ω—å, –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–≤—à–∏—Å—å —Å –¥–µ–ª–∞–º–∏, –æ–Ω –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–ª—Å—è –¥–æ–º–æ–π –∏–∑ –§—Ä–∞–Ω—Ü–∏–∏. –ë—ã–ª –ø–æ–∑–¥–Ω–∏–π –∑–∏–º–Ω–∏–π –≤–µ—á–µ—Ä. –£–≤–µ—à–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –ø–æ–¥–∞—Ä–æ—á–Ω—ã–º–∏ –ø–∞–∫–µ—Ç–∞–º–∏, —Å–≤–µ—Ç—è—Å—å, –∫–∞–∫ –∑–∞–∂–∂–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –Ω–æ–≤–æ–≥–æ–¥–Ω—è—è –µ–ª–∫–∞, –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–π —Ä–∞–¥–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–ª –¥–≤–µ—Ä—å –∫–≤–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä—ã.
–°—Ç–∞—Ä–∞—è—Å—å —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å —Å—é—Ä–ø—Ä–∏–∑, –Ω–∞ —Ü—ã–ø–æ—á–∫–∞—Ö –ø–æ–¥–æ—à–µ–ª –∫ –¥–≤–µ—Ä–∏ –∫–æ–º–Ω–∞—Ç—ã, –æ—Ç–∫—É–¥–∞ –ª–∏–ª–∞—Å—å —Ç–∏—Ö–∞—è –∑–Ω–∞–∫–æ–º–∞—è –º–µ–ª–æ–¥–∏—è.
‚Äì –ê –≤–æ—Ç –∏‚Ä¶ ‚Äì —Ä–∞–¥–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª –æ–Ω –∏ –æ—Å–µ–∫—Å—è.

‚Äì –ê —á—Ç–æ –º–Ω–µ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å? –í–µ–¥—å –µ–≥–æ –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–æ –¥–æ–º–∞! –£ –Ω–µ–≥–æ –≤ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–µ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–¥–∏–Ω –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å. –ê —è –∂–µ–Ω—â–∏–Ω–∞, –º–Ω–µ —Ç–µ–ø–ª–æ, –º–Ω–µ –ª–∞—Å–∫–∞ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–∞!
–ù–∞ —Ç–æ–º –æ–Ω–∏ –∏ —Ä–∞—Å—Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏—Å—å. –û—Å—Ç–∞–≤—à–∏—Å—å —É —Ä–∞–∑–±–∏—Ç–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ—Ä—ã—Ç–∞, –ù–∞—Ç–∞—à–∫–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–ª–∞ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—É—é –µ–π –∫–≤–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä—É –∏ –æ–±—Ä–µ—á–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —É–∫–∞—Ç–∏–ª–∞ –∫ –º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∏ –≤ –û–¥–µ—Å—Å—É.
–†–µ—à–∏–≤ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ —Ç—è–∂–µ–ª–æ–µ –±—Ä–µ–º—è –º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –µ–π –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–¥ —Å–∏–ª—É, –æ–Ω–∞ –¥–æ–≤–æ–ª—å–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–æ—Ä–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–ª–∞ –∏—Ö —á–µ—Ç—ã—Ä–Ω–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç–∏–ª–µ—Ç–Ω—é—é –¥–æ—á—å –≤ –æ–¥–∏–Ω –∏–∑ –≤–∞—Ä—à–∞–≤—Å–∫–∏—Ö –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–¥–∂–µ–π. –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω—É —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –ø–æ–≤–æ—Ä–æ—Ç —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏–π –±—ã–ª —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω–∞ —Ä—É–∫—É. –í —Å–ª–æ–∂–∏–≤—à–µ–π—Å—è —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ —Å—É–¥ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–∑–Ω–∞—á–Ω–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞–ª –æ–ø–µ–∫—É –Ω–∞–¥ —Ä–µ–±–µ–Ω–∫–æ–º –±—ã–≤—à–µ–π –∂–µ–Ω–µ, —É—á–µ–±–∞ –Ω–∞—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏—Ü—ã –≤ –ø—Ä–µ—Å—Ç–∏–∂–Ω–æ–º –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–¥–∂–µ –±—ã–ª–∞ –∫—É–¥–∞ –ª—É—á—à–µ, —á–µ–º –±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–Ω–æ–µ –æ—Ç—Ä–æ—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –Ω–∞ –ú–∞–ª–æ–π –ê—Ä–Ω–∞—É—Ç—Å–∫–æ–π. –ù–µ–¥–æ–ª–≥–æ –¥—É–º–∞—è, –æ–Ω –æ–ø–ª–∞—Ç–∏–ª –æ–±—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–æ—á–µ—Ä–∏ –∑–∞ –≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü–µ–π.
–ù–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º–µ—Å—è—Ü–µ–≤ —Å–∫–∏—Ç–∞—è—Å—å –ø–æ —á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω—ã–º –∫–≤–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–º, –°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–π —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —É–≤–∏–ª–∏–≤–∞–ª –æ—Ç –Ω–∞–≤—è–∑—á–∏–≤–æ–π –∑–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã –±–ª–∏–∑–∫–∏—Ö. –ò—Ö –∏–∑–ª–∏—à–Ω–µ–µ –ø–æ–ø–µ—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–µ —à–ª–æ –µ–º—É –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É. –ü–µ—Ä–µ–µ—Ö–∞–≤ –∫ —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è–º –≤ –ò—Ä–ø–µ–Ω—å, –æ–Ω —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –∑–∞–º–µ—Ç–∏–ª, —á—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –µ–≥–æ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–º —Ä–µ–º–Ω–µ –∏–∑ –±–ª–µ—Å—Ç—è—â–µ–π –∫—Ä–æ–∫–æ–¥–∏–ª—å–µ–π –∫–æ–∂–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –Ω–µ —Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –¥—ã—Ä–æ–∫. –í–µ–¥—å –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ã–º –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–Ω—ã–º –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º –µ–≥–æ –º–∞—Ç—É—à–∫–∏ –±—ã–ª–æ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–æ–µ –∂–µ–ª–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞–∫–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ç—å ¬´—Ä–µ–±–µ–Ω–∫–∞¬ª –≤—Å–µ–≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Ä–∞–∑–Ω–æ—Å–æ–ª–∞–º–∏ –∏ —Å–¥–æ–±–æ–π. –ê —Ç–∞–∫ –∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∏–∫—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –∑–µ–º–ª–µ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å –ª—É—á—à–µ –Ω–µ–µ, —Ç–æ —Å–∏–ª—ã —É–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –æ—Ç –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–µ–π –ª–æ–∂–∫–∏ –í–æ–ª–æ—à–∏–Ω –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª –Ω–µ –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞. –ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É, –ø—Ä–∏–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞—è—Å—å —Ç–≤–µ—Ä–¥–æ–≥–æ —É–±–µ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è, —á—Ç–æ –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–º —É –º—É–∂—á–∏–Ω—ã –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∫–æ—à–µ–ª–µ–∫ –∏ —Å—á–µ—Ç –≤ –±–∞–Ω–∫–µ, –æ–Ω –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è–ª —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ —É–¥—Ä–∞—Ç—å –∏–∑-–ø–æ–¥ —Å—Ç–æ–ª—å –≥—É–±–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–π –æ–ø–µ–∫–∏. –°–æ—Å–ª–∞–≤—à–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∏—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ–∑–¥–Ω–æ –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–æ–º–æ–π, —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ —Ç—Ä–µ–≤–æ–∂–∏—Ç—å —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π –Ω–æ—á–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∑–≤–æ–Ω–∫–∞–º–∏ –∏ –ø–æ–¥–æ–ª–≥—É –¥–æ–±–∏—Ä–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–æ –ö–∏–µ–≤–∞, –æ–Ω —Å–±–µ–∂–∞–ª –Ω–∞ –∫–≤–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä—É –∫ —Å–≤–æ–µ–º—É –¥–∞–≤–Ω–µ–º—É –¥—Ä—É–≥—É –∏ –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω—å–æ–Ω—É –î–∏–º–∫–µ –ö–æ—Ä–Ω–∏–µ–Ω–∫–æ.

Farriin Barkulannada Bulshada Lagu Baahiyo Ayaa Dunida Wax Ka Beddeli Karta. Qisadan Ayaa Tusaale Ah (1)
Washington (Geeska)- Dad badan ayaa dhayalsada saamaynta ay yeelan karaan farriimaha lagu baahiyo barkulannada bulshada ee internet ka, laakiin waxaa laga yaabaa in uu fikirkoodaasi is beddelo haddii ay dhugtaan qisaska laga sheego saamynta ay farriimo lagu baahiyey barkulannada bulshadu ku yeesheen dunida, ee dhinaca siyaasadda, dhaqaalaha iyo bulshadaba leh.
Maqaaxida caalamiga ah ee MacDonalds ayaa barta ay ku leedahay shabakadda Twitter ka waxa ay ku faafisay farriin ay ku sheegayso in Beergarrada (Burger) ay samayso nooc ka mid ah oo lagu magacaabo ‚ÄòQuarter Pounder‚Äô, ‚ÄúIllaa badhtamaha sannadka 2018-ka, laga samayn doonaa hilib lo‚Äôaad oo daray ah‚Äù In kasta oo ay shirkaddani arrintan xayeysiis uga jeedday, waxaa ku soo baxay jawaab aanay filayn oo weliba ka timid hudheelka kale ee uu tartanku ka dhexeeyo ee WENDYS oo isagana xaruntiisu tahay dalka Maraykanka laakiin laamo ku leh meelo badan oo dunida ka mid ah. WENDY‚ÄôS oo caan ku ah in uu boggiisa twitter kaftan iyo ilaaq ku haasaawiyo macaamiishiisa, ayaa McDonalds ugu jawaabay, ‚ÄúMarkaa macnuhu waxa weeye in hilib aan daray ahayn ay u isticmaali doonaan inta badan ee beergarradooda kale, hudheelladooda oo dhan‚Äù
WENDYS in kasta oo ay McDonalds ku jiqsiisay, laakiin iyaduna kama ay faa‚Äôidin farriintan oo waxaa meel dhow kaga soo baxay wiil dhalinyaro ah oo u heellan in uu cuntadooda bilaash ku cuno, ‚ÄúImisa jeer marka aan dib u soo celiyo farriintiinan ‚ÄòRetweet‚Äô ayaa aan muddo sannad ah bilaa lacag ku cunayaa digaagga aad samaysaan nooca wasladaha ah‚Äù ayaa uu wiilkan oo la yidhaahdo Carter Wilkerson u soo qoray hudheelkan isaga oo ugu duur-xulaya in sababta ay farriinta u soo dhigeenba tahay in dadku ay marar badan soo celceliyaan.
Hudheelka WENDYS su‚Äôaashan waa uu ka baxsaday oo waxa uu wiilkan u soo qoray, farriin jawaab ah oo uu doonayo in uu ku gudhiyo damaciisa, waxa aanu si xaqiraad ah ugu soo qoray, ‚Äú18 Milyan oo jeer marka aad ku celiso‚Äù
Wiilkani kuma uu joogsan carinta hudheelka ee waxa uu bilaabay dagaal dheer oo uu ku suurtogelinayo in uu gaadho 18-ka milyan ee cod ee uu hudheelku soo dhigay isaga oo u haysta in aanu gaadhi karin. Hal Maalin oo keliya ayaa uu Carter ku kasbaday 1 Milyan oo jawaab celinood ‚ÄòRetweet‚Äô waa uu sii waday illaa farriintii WENDYS ay ka mid noqotay farriinta labaad ee dadkii ugu badnaa abid ku faafiyaan bogga twitter ka, laakiin weli ma‚Äô uu ka hadhin ee waa uu sii waday, waxa aanu gaadhay 3.2 Milyan oo jeer in lagu celiyey ‚ÄòRetweet‚Äô
Haddii uu Carter arrintan ku doonayey digaag bilaa lacag ah oo uu hal sano cuno, arrintii waa ay ka sii weynaatay oo shirkado waaweyn ayaa bogaggooda twitter ka dib ugu celiyey farriintiisa ‚ÄòRetweet‚Äô si ay xayeysiis ahaan uga faa‚Äôidaystaan malaayiinta qof ee ku xidhan farriintan, waxaa shirkadahaas ka mid ah, Amazon, Microsoft, Twitter lafteeda iyo Google oo xitaa mar ereyga calaamadda u ah ee GOOGLE xarfaha uu ka kooban yahay u ekeysiisay hilib digaag.
Shirkaddii WENDEYS ee marka hore farriinta u soo dhigtay in ay wiilkan ku niyadjebiso ayaa mark ale ku soo noqotay farriintii oo ku dhawaaqday in haddii dadka dib ugu celinaya farriintaasi ‚ÄòRetweet‚Äô ay farriinta gaadhsiiyaan in ay noqoto tii ugu shacbiyadda badnayd taariikhda Twitter in hudheelkoodu uu 100 kun oo doolar ugu deeqayo hay‚Äôadda Dave Thomas Foundation oo ka shaqaysa daryeelka agoonta iyo in ubadka aan cidda lahayn u raadiso cid korsata.
Arrintani xamaasaddii ayaa ay sii kordhisay oo farriintii Carter waxa ee hal-ku-dheggeedu ahaa ‚Äú#NuggsforCarter‚Äù ayaa gaadhay 64 Milyan oo jeer in lagu celiyo. Halkaa kuma ay joogsan, ee shirkadda kale ee Oath ayaa ku dhawaaqday in ay iyaduna 100 kun oo kale ku bixin doonto tabaruca hay‚Äôaddaas, haddii farriinta Carter ay noqoto ta ugu shacbiyadda badan ee abid twitter soo martay.
Marka aynu soo koobna farriinta lagu faafiyey barkulanka bulsho waxa ay sababtay in dad badani faa‚Äôiidaan, hudheelkii WENDYS magac iyo xayeysiis ayaa uu ka faa‚Äôiiday oo mar kasta shaashadaha ka warramaya farriintan xawliga ku faafaysa ayaa xusayey magaciisa. Hay‚Äôaddaas samofalkuna waxa ay ka faa‚Äôiiday 200 oo kun oo doolar. Halka Carter oo ah wiilka bilaabay uu isku darsaday, casho bilaash ah iyo in uu noqdo shakhsi caan ah, oo warbaahintu waraysiyo iyo kulamo tiro badan la yeelato.

Wasiirka arimaha dibadda dalkan Norway B√∏rge Brende ayaa bisha soo socoto isaga dagi doono xilka wasiirnimo, kadib markii loo magacaabay inuu noqdo madaxweynaha madasha dhaqaalaha iyo jeeb-weynayaasha aduunka ee World Economic Forum.
Reysulwasaaraha Norway Erna Solberg oo Brende ay isku xisbi yihiin iyo gudoomiyaha xisbiga shaqaalaha Jonas Gahr St√∏rre ayaa labuduba hambalyo u diray wasiirka xilka kasii dagi rabo.
Brende ayaa agaasime ka ahaa madasha WEF intii u dhaxeysay 2008-2009, isaga maamulaha guud isla madashaas ka noqday sanadkii 2011, wuxuuna xilkaa hayay ilaa 2013 markaas oo Erna Solberg ay u magacowday wasiirka arimaha dibada dalkan Norway.
Brende ayaa magaalada Muqdisho booqasho ku tagay sanadkan 2017, isaga oo halkaas kula kulmay madaxda dowlada federaalka ah ee Soomaaliya, wuxuuna ahaa masuulkii ugu sareeyay ee Norwiiji ah ee Soomaaliya booqasho ku tago mudo sanado ah. Bishii May ayuu sidoo kale magaalada Doha kula kulmay reysulwasaaraha Soomaaliya, Hassan Ali Kheyre.
Wasiirka arimaha dibada Norway oo maanta Muqdisho ka dagay Wasiirka arimaha dibada Norway oo hambalyo u diray madaxweynaha cusub ee Soomaaliya Wasiirka arimaha dibada Soomaaliya iyo Gaafow oo safar shaqo ku joogo Norwey Yuusuf Garaad(wasiirka A. Dibada Somaliya) oo kulan la qaadan doono jaaliyada soomaaliyeed ee Norway

Xukun lagu riday odaygii ku soo caanbaxay kufsiga ...
Xukun lagu riday odaygii ku soo caanbaxay kufsiga - Radio Sweden Somali - Raadiyaha Iswiidhen | Sveriges Radio
Xukun lagu riday odaygii ku soo caanbaxay kufsiga
La daabacay tisdag 9 april 2013 kl 13.23
Maanta ayey maxkamadda degmadu xukun ku riday ninkii ku caanbaxay magaca S√∂dermannen. Waxaa lagu soo eedeeyey in uu galmo aan khasab ahayn la sameeyey gabar ay nolosha dhibaato ka haysatay. Waxaa dhacdaan loo arkaa in ay tahay kufsi ilmo yar maadaama ay gabadhani markaas jirtay 14 sano. Ninkani wuxuu gabadha siiyey daroogada loo yaqaan cannabis si uu u la galmoodo.
Maxkamadda degmada ayaa ninkaan ku xukuntay in uu galay falal dembi oo kala ah i uu kufsaday dhallaan, in uu dhallaan ka iibsaday la galmood iyo dembi daroogo la xiriira. Ciqaabtuna waxay noqotay afar sano oo xabsi ah.
Ninkaan ayaa horay loogu xukumay falal kufsi oo is dabajoog ah oo ka dhacay magaalooyinka G√∂teborg iyo Stockholm sanooyinkii toddobaatanadii iyo siddeetameeyadii. Waayadaas wuxuu gurigiisa u soo kaxaysan jirey dumar uu kadibna kufsan jirey.

Gabadhii astaanta u noqotay dibadbaxyada Suudaan o...
Gabadhii astaanta u noqotay dibadbaxyada Suudaan oo tusaale xun usoo qaadatay Soomaaliya |
Gabadhii astaanta u noqotay dibadbaxyada Suudaan oo tusaale xun usoo qaadatay Soomaaliya
Bar Twitter oo la sheegay in ay leedahay Alaa Saalax oo ah gabadh reer Suudaan ah oo ka mid aheyd dadkii horkacayay dibadbaxyada galaaftay madaxweynihii hore ee Suudaan, Cumar Xasan Al-Bashiir, ayaa barteeda Twitter-ka kusoo qortay erey ay dad badan dhibsadeen.
Waxay sheegtay in xaaladda Suudaan aysan la mid aheyn midda ka taagan dalka Soomaaliya.
‚ÄúRa‚Äôiisul wasaaraha Itoobiya Abiy Axmed waxaa uu soo gaaray Khartuum, booqasho lagu tilmaamay dhexdhexaadinta dibadbaxyaasha Suudaan iyo hoggaamiyeyaasha militariga. Suudaan ma ahan sida Soomaaliya,‚Äù ayay tiri Alaa Saalax.
Lama xaqiijin karo bartan in ay Alaa Saalax leedahay balse dad badan ayaa si kala duwan uga falceliyay farriinta lagu qoray.
Qaar kamid ah dadka Soomaalida ee adeegsada baraha bulshada ayaa ka carooday qoraalka Alaa Saalax oo ay ku sheegeen mid aanan habooneyn isla markaasna shacabka deggan labada dal ay yihiin dad walaalo ah.
Waxay ay sheegeen in Soomaalida ay qaddariyaan shacabka reer Suudaan oo aysan ku jeesjeesin.
Sidoo kale qaar ka mid ah dadka isticmaala Twitter-ka ayaa ugu baaqay gabadhan in sharaftii geesinimada aheyd ay ku hanatay kacdoonka, aysan si khaldan u adeegsan oo aysan ku weerarin dad gaar ah oo horey u taageeray.
Dadka soomaalida waxay taageersan yihiin isbaddallada ka dhacay Suudaan balse ‚Äúma aheyn in Alaa ay so qorto aflagaado ka dhan ah Soomaaliya‚Äù.
Markii uu dalkaasi ka socday kacdoonkii looga soo horjeeday dowladda Al-Bashiir, waxaa baraha bulshada qabsaday Alaa oo qaadaysa hees lagu tageerayo kacdoonka iyada oo gaari dusha ka saaran oo dibad baxayaal badanna ay hareero taagnaayeen.
Sawirka wakhtigaas laga qaaday ayaana astaan u noqday kacdoonka maalmihii u dambeeyay maamulkii Cumar Xasan Al-Bashiir.
Alaa Saalax
Alaa Saalax, gabadhii hormuudka ka noqotay kacdoonkii lagu afgembiyay madaxweynihii Suudaan Cumar Xassan Al Bashiir. Maxay isu aragtaa iyada?.
Sl√•et op af BBC News Somali i Fredag den 26. april 2019

DEG DEG: Itoobiya oo ku dhawaaqday qabashada xubno...
DEG DEG: Itoobiya oo ku dhawaaqday qabashada xubno katirsanaa DAACISH.
September 11, 2019 puntlandtimes 0
ADDIS ABABA(P-TIMES) ‚Äì Taliska guud ee ciidamada Difaaca dalka Itoobiya ayaa ku dhawaaqay in ay qabteen qaar kamid ah ama dad ka tirsanaa kooxda la baxday dawladda Islaamiga ah ee loo yaqaano ISIS, kuwaas oo dhawaan ku hanjabay in ay falal Argagixiso ka geysa doonaan gudaha dalka Itoobiya.
Sidda laga baahiyey warbaahinta dawladda Itoobiya waxaa la qabtay oo la xiray qaar kamid ah dagaalamayasha kooxdaas oo isku dayay in ay falal amaan darro ka geystaan gudaha Itoobiya, waxaana ay hadda sugayaan in maxkamaddaha la horgeeyo.
Taliye kuxigeenka guud ee ciidanka Itoobiya ahna Madaxa Howlgalada Jeneraal Berhanu Jula ayaa warkan shaaciyey, wuxuuna sheegay in ay wali dabagal ku hayaan wararka iyo arrimaha la xariira kooxdan oo dhawaan hanjabaad u dirtay Addis Ababa.
Jeneraal Berhanu wuxuu sheegay in ay ciidamada Qaranka Itoobiya ka shaqeynayaan sidii looga shaqeyn lahaa nabadgalyada dalka, isagoo sheegay in ay wax kasta oo dhibaato ah ka hortagi doonaan oo ay gacan bir ah ku qabanayaan.
Madaxa howlgalada ayaa sheegay in ay marar badan kooxdan ISIS isku dayday in ay ficilo ka fuliso gudaha Itoobiya, oo ay dib u soo galiyeen gudaha dad lasoo tababaray, kuwa la shaqaaleysiiyey iyo xataa agabyo kala duwan oo ay hayaan ciidamada Amnigu kana hortageen.
Wargeyska New Age ee kasooo baxa Addis Ababa ayaa daabacay wareysi dheer uu layeeshay Taliye kuxigeenka ciidamada Itoobiya oo shaaciyey in ay dabagal ku hayaan wax kasta oo la xariira macluumaadka kooxaha Argagixiso.
Kooxda la baxday dawladda Islaamiga ah ee ISIS waxay dhawaan shaacisay in ay weeraro ka geysan doonto gudaha Itoobiya, taas oo loo arkayay khatar weyn oo gobalka kusoo siyaaday, balse ma jirin jawaab rasmi ah oo ay dawladda Addis Ababa ka bixisay arrimahan, inkastoo qabashada iyo dhawaaqa cusub ee ciidamaddu uu hadda daaha ka rogayo in kooxahaas la fashiliyey.

CALI GADHEER OO SIILAANYO U XILSAARAY WAREEJINTA H...
CALI GADHEER OO SIILAANYO U XILSAARAY WAREEJINTA HAAMAHA MUDDO BIL AHNA KU SUGNAAN DOONA BERBERA | Saxil News Network
CALI GADHEER OO SIILAANYO U XILSAARAY WAREEJINTA HAAMAHA MUDDO BIL AHNA KU SUGNAAN DOONA BERBERA
Berbera ( saxilnews.com)-Madaxweynaha mudo-xileedkii la doortay dhamaaday ee Axmad Siilaanyo ayaa intaanu saaka dalka ka dhoofin wasiir-ku xigeenkii Xanaanada Xoolaha Cali Gadheer u magacaabay xil dheeraad ah oo uu ku noqanayo Wakiilka xukuumadda ee Wareejinta Haamaha Keydka Shidaalka ee Berbera.Cali Gadheer ayaa waxa Mr Siilaanyo faray inuu ku sugnaado magaalada Berbera muddo bil ah si uu u hirgaliyo isla markaana taabogal ka dhigo qorshaha xukuumaddu ku doonayso inay Haamaha u gacangaliso wasiiro iyada ka tirsan iyo shakhsiyad awood leh oo ku xidhan madaxtooyada kuwaaso sheeganaya inay shirkado yihiin.
Cali Gadheer oo hadda ku sugan Berbera ayaa marki uu qorshaha dawladda ee Haamaha khuseeya uu soo shaacbaxay waxa uu dad badan oo reer Berbera ah u sheegay inuu ka soo horjeedo wareejinta laakiin waxa la ogaaday inuu is-rogay markii ay isaga iyo wasiir ku-xigeenka Ganacsiga Cali Dhagoole ay todobvaadkii hore shir jaraayid oo ay Hargeysa ku qabteen ku muujiyeen inay taageersanyihiin wareejinta Haamaha.Waliba Cali Dhagoole ayaa shirkaasi jaraayid waxa uu ka jeediyey hadalo hanjabaad iyo aflagaado isugu jiray oo uu si gaar ah ugu maagayey reer Berbera iyadoo ay jirto in mucaaradada wareejinta Haamuhu ay asalkeedii hore ka bilaabantay caasimadda Hargeysa kadibna Somaliland oo dhan wada saameysay.Cali Dhagoole oo haatan u muuqda nin inta lagu shaqeystay dabadeed la tuuray ayaa waxay kala dhex miiranaysa Cali Gadheer.
Dhinaca kale arinta wareejinta Haamaha ayaa waxa laga cabsi qabaa inay keento isku-dhac dhex mara dadweynaha reer Berbera iyo ciidamada ay xukuumaddu halkaasi soo dhoobtay iyadoo ay saan saan jawi colaadeed oo shabahda tii 1992/93 ay ka muuqato magaalada, xili dareenka dadkuna aad u kacsanyahay oo bulshada ku dhaqan Berberina ay hadda ka mideysan tahay kana soo horjeeddo wareejinta Haamaha

Madaxweyne Muuse Biixi Oo Ka Qayb-galay Aas Qaran ...
Madaxweyne Muuse Biixi Oo Ka Qayb-galay Aas Qaran Oo Loo Sameeyey Marxuum Axmed Yuusuf | ToggaHerer

Qaraxyo ka dhacay Dhuusamareeb iyo Al Shabaab oo sheegatay Mas‚Äôuuliyadda ‚Üí
Hargeysa-14-07-2019-(THN)-Madaxweynaha Jamhuuriyadda Somaliland, Mudane Muuse Biixi Cabdi, ayaa maanta ka qayb-galay Aas qaran oo xabaalaha Xaraf ee duleedka caasimadda Hargeysa loogu sameeyey marxuum Axmed Yuusuf Siciid oo kamid ahaa haldoorka miisaanka ku leh dhex bulshada reer Somaliland, dhawaanna ku geeriyooday dalka Ingiriiska.

KULMIYE Party ¬ª Dhallinyarada iyo Aqoonyahanka Bee...
KULMIYE Party ¬ª Dhallinyarada iyo Aqoonyahanka Beesha Abokor Muuse (Ciidagale) oo Taageero u Muujiyey Xisbiga KULMIYE Dhallinyarada iyo Aqoonyahanka Beesha Abokor Muuse (Ciidagale) oo Taageero u Muujiyey Xisbiga KULMIYE ‚Äì KULMIYE Party
Dhallinyarada iyo Aqoonyahanka Beesha Abokor Muuse (Ciidagale) oo Taageero u Muujiyey Xisbiga KULMIYE
HomeDhallinyarada iyo Aqoonyahanka Beesha Abokor Muuse (Ciidagale) oo Taageero u Muujiyey Xisbiga KULMIYE
Hargeysa(Warbaahinta Xisbiga KULMIYE)-Dhallinyarada, aqoonyahanka, waxgaradka iyo siyaasiyiinta beesha Abokor Muuse oo kamid ah beelweynta Ciidagale, ayaa si rasmi ah u muujisay cududooda taageero ee ay u hayaan xisbiga KULMIYE iyo murrashaxiintiisa.
Munaasibad ay dhallnyarada, aqoonyahanka, waxgaradka iyo siyaasiyiinta beeshani ku muujinayso taageerada ay KULMIYE u hayaan oo xalay lagu qabtay hutel Gacalle ee magaalada Hargeysa, isla markaana ay ka qaybgaleen hormoodka iyo haldoorka beesha iyo xubno xilal muhiim ah ka haya xisbiga KULMIYE iyo xukuumadda oo ay kamid yihiin wasiiru-dawlaha wasaaradda Biyaha Md.Cabdiqaadir Sheekh Maxamuud Muxumed (Dhego-weyne), xildhibaan Cabdiraxmaan Cismaan Caalin, xildhibaan Axmed Siyaad Muxumed, guddoomiyaha xisbiga KULMIYE ee gobolka Maroodi-jeex Md. Maxamed Iid Dhimbiil, maareeye ku-xigeenka wakaallada Biyaha Hargeysa, dhallinyaro, aqoonyahan, haween iyo marti-sharaf tiro badan, ayaa lagu shaaciyey inay beeshani si rasmi ah u taageersan tahay xisbiga KULMIYE iyo murrashaxiintiisa.
Xubnihii madasha ka hadlay, ayaa si isku mid ah u shaaciyey inay beel ahaan ka siman yihiin taageerada xisbiga KULMIYE, isla markaana ay codkooda si hagar la‚Äôaan ah u siin doonaan murrashaxiinta madaxweynaha iyo ku-xigeenka ugu tartamaya xisbiga KULMIYE.
Haldoorka, siyaasiyiinta iyo waxgaradka beesha Abokor Muuse oo hadalka u kala dambeeyey, ayaa si qoto dheer u sharraxay xidhiidhka ma guuraanka ah ee beesha iyo xisbiga KULMIYE u dhexeeya, waxana ay murrashaxiinta xisbiga ugu bushaareeyeen inay codkooda iyo taageeradoodaba ku xisaabtamaan.
Wasiiru-dawlaha wasaaradda Biyaha Md.Cabdiqaadir Sheekh Maxamuud Muxumed oo isagu soo abaabulay munaaswibadda taageerada ah, isla markaana safka hore kaga jira dedaalka loogu jiro sidii uu xisbiga KULMIYE markale talada dalka ugu guulaysan lahaa oo isaguna halkaas ka hadlay, ayaa tilmaamay inay beel ahaan ka midaysan yihiin taageerada KULMIYE.
Xildhibaan Cabdiraxmaan Cismaan Caalin oo kamid ah mudaneyaasha xisbiga KULMIYE ugu jira aqalka golaha wakiillada, ayaa isaguna sheegay inuu xisbiga KULMIYE taageero ballaadhan ku dhex leeyahay beesha Abokor Muuse, kuwaas oo dhalin kara guul uu xisbiga KULMIYE gaadho.
Taageerada ay dhallinyarada, aqoonyahanka iyo siyaasiyiinta beesha Abokor Muuse u muujiyeen xisbiga KULMIYE, ayaa kusoo beegantay xilli ay waxgaradka beelo badan oo reer Somaliland ahi sidan oo kale u muujiyeen taageerada ay KULMIYE u hayaan, waxana ay tallaabadani ka marag kacaysaa sida uu xisbigu kaabiga ugu hayo inuu guul ballaadhan kassoo hooyo doorashooyinka soo socda.

Haala uummatani Oromoo keessa jiru dhugumatti huba...
Haala uummatani Oromoo keessa jiru dhugumatti hubannee jirraa? ¬´ QEERROO
December 10, 2017 By Qeerroo in Oduu/News	Leave a comment
Sochiin uummata Oromoo, kan bara 2014 irraa eegalee godhamaa jiru kun injifannoo hawwame dafee argamsiisuu baatullee, jijjiirama addaa addaa argamsiisaa jira. Mooraa diinotaa keessatti naasuu guddaa mul‚Äôisee jira. OPDOn yookaanis hoggantootni ishii gadi bahanii jechoota Sabboonummaa fi Oromummaa addeessan akka haasa‚Äôan taasisee jira. Waan haasa‚Äôaa jiran kana hojiidhaan ni agarsiisu jedhee ani garuu hin yaadu. Biyya alaatti ammoo aktivistootni akka wacan godhee jira. Haala kana keessatti xiinxaltootni fi beektotnis heddoomanii jiru. Abbaan malaa fi falaa nuyi jechaa ofmumul‚Äôisaa jiru. Tooftaa fi tarsiimoo yeroon gaafattu isa kana ykn sana jechaa dubbachaa fi barreessaa jiru. Addunyaa jabaadhaaf malee laafadhaaf gurra hin kenninetti iyyachaa jiru. Wanti mul‚Äôachaa jiru tarreen isaa dheeraa dha. Garuu tokkumtillee uummata Oromoo yeroo ammaa yoomiyyuu caalaa haala baay‚Äôee hamaa keessa jiru gargaaruu waan danda‚Äôe natti hin fakkaatu.
Dhugaa dha, wanti dagatamuu hin qabne uummata keenya kan naannoo Somaaleerraa buqifamaniif gargaarsi guddaan godhamee jira. Kun akka laayyootti ilaalamuu hin qabu. Warri isa kana keessatti gahee taphatani fi qooda gumaachan galanni isaanii guddaa dha. Dirqama Oromummaa fi lammummaa baatanii jirtuu, ulfaadhaa jechuun barbaada. Haa ta‚Äôu malee, wanti godhaman hunduu akkuma jiranitti ta‚Äôanii, wanti gaafii natti ta‚Äôu dhugumatti haala uummatni keenya keessa jiru sirriitti hubannee jirraa? Hanguma sochiin uummataa jabaachaa deemu, diinnis tooftaalee fi tarsiimoolee adda addaatti fayyadamuudhaan lola cimaa nurratti godhaa jira, godhuufis deema. Kun waanuma hubatamaa jiru fi hunduu beekuu danda‚Äôan waan ta‚Äôeef, asirratti bal‚Äôinaan ibsuu hin barbaachisu. Qabiyyeen barreeffama kanaas gabaasa haala yeroo dhiyeessuufii miti.
Barreeffama gabaabaa kana akkan dhiyeessu kan na taasisan waan tibbana babarreeffamaa jiranii dha. Isaan kana keessaa waa lamatu qalbii kiyya hawwatan. Inni tokko barreeffama mata duree ‚ÄúOromiyaa walaboomtu moo Federeeshinii dhugaa: Galii siyaasaa isa kamtu Oromoof wayya?‚Äù jedhuun Berhanu Hundeetiin dhiyaate http://ayyaantuu.net/oromiyaa-walaboomtu-moo-federeeshinii-dhugaa/ yoo ta‚Äôu; inni biraa ammoo barreeffama kanaaf deebii kennuuf mata duree ‚ÄúGaaffii Siyaasaa Oromoof Wayyu: Walabummaa Oromiyaa‚Äù jedhuun Luuccee Gurmuutiin dhiyaate http://ayyaantuu.net/gaaffii-siyaasaa-oromoof-wayyu-walabummaa-oromiyaa/ dha. Barreeffama lamaanuu dubbisee, hamma naa galetti hubachuu yaalee jira. Akka ilaalcha fi hubannoo kiyyaatitti, garaagarummaan barruulee lameen kana jidduu jiru baay‚Äôee xiqqaa dha.
Garaagarummaan kun maali yoo jedhame, Luuccee Gurmuu ejjannoo ifa ta‚Äôe akka qabu fi asirraayis ka‚Äôee furmaatni siyaasaa Oromoof ta‚Äôu isa kana qofaa dha jedhee Walabummaa Oromiyaa akka galii xumuraatti lafa kaayuu dha. Dabalataan ammoo, barreeffamni biraas kan Luuccee Gurmuutiin Afaan Ingiliziitiin dhiyaate ‚ÄúA Better Alternative for the Oromo: Independent State of Oromia‚Äù http://ayyaantuu.net/independent-state-oromia/ jedhu ejjannoo isaa ifa godha. Karaa faallaatiin yoo ilaalame ammoo, barreeffamni Berhanu Hundee kan mul‚Äôisu, gama tokkoon, Federeeshiniin dhugaa yoo mirkanaaye inni kun Oromoof badaa akka hin taanee dha; yoo haal dureen inni barreeffama isaa keessatti tuqe guutame jechuu natti fakkaata. Gama biraatiin garuu, Berhanuun furmaatni Oromoof wayyu isa kana jedhee ifaa ifatti waan lafa kaaye natti hin fakkaatu. Erga gaafii kana kaasee, silaa innis furmaata ifa ta‚Äôe tokko ibsuutu irra ture; ejjannoo ifa ta‚Äôeen jechuu kooti. Egaa kun hubannoo ani barruulee lamaanirraa argadhee dha.
Gara mata duree barreeffama kanaatti deebi‚Äôuuf, haalli uummatni Oromoo keessa jiru yoomiyyuu caalaa hamaa kan ta‚Äôe; haala jiruu fi jireenya saba kanaa murteessu keessa jirra.Haala hamaa ta‚Äôe kana keessaa bahuuf ykn kufuuf karaa lama qofaatu jiru: yookaani yeroo xumuraatiif rakkoo keenyaaf furmaatin maayii argamee, akka sabaatti fi uummataatti jiraachuu yookaan ammoo badnee Addunyaa kanarraa dhabamuuf deemna jechuu dha. Yeroo xumuraatiif furmaata isa maayii yoon jedhu maal jechuu kiyya? Akkuman kanaan duras yeroo adda addaa fi barruulee adda addaa keessatti ibsuu yaalaa ture, ammas irradeebi‚Äôuuf, Oromiyaan walaboomtee; mootummaa birmadummaa yoo ijaarratte malee, biyyattii Itoophiyaa jedhamtu sana keessatti Oromon nagaa fi tasgabbii argatee jiraachuu hin danda‚Äôu jedheen amana. Kanaaf, gabaabumatti galii isa kanatu furmaata xumuraa ykn maayii ta‚Äôuu qaba jechuu dha.
Dugaa dha, wanti dhara hin taane, Haalli Gaafa Aafrikkas ta‚Äôee kan Addunyaa baay‚Äôee walxaxaa fi ulfaataa akka ta‚Äôe nan hubadha. Haala akkanaa kana keessatti furmaata xumuraa armaan olitti kaase argachuun hin danda‚Äôamu jedhanii warri morman jiraachuu akka malan shakkiin hin jiru. Waayee kana ammoo waanuma argaa fi dhagahaa as geenye fi ammas argaa jirru waan ta‚Äôeefi. Haa ta‚Äôu malee, wanti hunduu hubachuu qaban, dhugaan lafarratti mula‚Äôchaa jiru, Oromoon taa‚Äôus lolus; Itoophiyaa diimookraatessuuf falmatus; Oromiyaa walaboomtuuf qabsaa‚Äôus; kanas ta‚Äôee sana, du‚Äôuurraa hin oolle. Erga guyyaarraa gara guyyaatti du‚Äôuun hin oollee, maaliif wareegama hammamuu ulfaatu kaffalee furmaata xumuraa hin arganne? Oromiyaa walaboomtu arguun maaliif hin danda‚Äôamne? Addunyaa kanarra wanti hin danda‚Äôamne hin jiruu bar!!!
Yeroo ammaa yeroo yoomiyyuu caalaa uummatni keenya dammaqee ka‚Äôee; tokkummaa isaa cimsaa jiru kanatti; yeroo xumurri gabrummaa dhiyaachaa jirutti; kutannoo fi murannoodhaan gara galii xumuraatti deemuun barbaachisaa dha murteessaa dhas. Amma qabsoo cimsanii; Oromiyyaa walaboomtu argamsiisuu baannan carraan akkanaa yoomiyyuu hin argamu. Kanaaf, karaa danda‚Äôamu hundaan qabeenya, beekumsa, dandeettii fi humna keenya cimsinee; Impaayarittiin tun diigamtee; awwaalcha ishiirratti biyya Gadaa Repabiliika Oromiyaa ijaaruu dha. Kanaa ala galiin biraa Oromoof nagaa fiduu akka hin dandeenye, kan Waaqni agarsiisu arguu danda‚Äôa. Yoomiyyuu haa ta‚Äôuu, injifannoon xumuraa garuu kan uummata keenyaa akka ta‚Äôu shakkiin hin jiru.

Abdirashid Ismail oo Maqaal Xiiso Leh Ka Qoray Xii...
Abdirashid Ismail oo Maqaal Xiiso Leh Ka Qoray Xiisadda Ka Dhalatay Mowshinka Madaxwayaha ka dhanka. | gobannimo
Home MAQAALO Abdirashid Ismail oo Maqaal Xiiso Leh Ka Qoray Xiisadda Ka Dhalatay Mowshinka...
Abdirashid Ismail oo Maqaal Xiiso Leh Ka Qoray Xiisadda Ka Dhalatay Mowshinka Madaxwayaha ka dhanka.
Abdirashid Ismail oo kamid ah dhallinyarada Soomaaliyeed ee aqoonyahannada ah, inta bandanna qormo iyo falanqayn ka sameeya arrimaha ay tahay in bulsahda lala wadaago ayaa qormo xiiso badan waxa uu ka sameeyay mowshinka laga gudbiyayy Madaxwayne maxamed Cabdullaahi Maxamed (Farmaajo).
Abdirashid Ismail ayaa bartiisa facebook soo dhigay qormara oo uu ku billaabay qiimaynta xaaladda, kooxda mas‚Äôuuliyadda leh, waxa uuna qaybta dambe uu qoraalkiisa ku gudbiyay talooyin muhiim u ah hay‚Äôadaha dawladda.
Hoos Ka aqri Maqaalka
Marka aan qiimeeyay sida wax u socdaan, khilaafka u dhaxeeya Gudoomiye Mursal iyo Laanta fulinta, arrimaha leeysku hayo ee kala ah doorshada Baydhabo iyo sii shaqeeynta guddiga Maaliyadda ee Baarlamaanka, sharcininada go‚Äôaanki kala dirista Guddiga ee ay gaareen Gudoomiye ku xigeenada Baarlamaanka.
Marka aan daraaseeyay, aqriyay qodobbada dastuuriga ah ee ku qoran warqadda eedda ama motionka ay soo gudbiyeen Xildhibaanadau.
Tirada Xildhibaanada ku saxiixan oo ah hal garab (damul jadiid).
Arrimahaas oo dhan markaan falanqeeyay, Wax cusub iima muuqdaan. Sababtuna waxeey tahay, Xildhibaanada 92 ah waan ogeeyn ineey mucaard yihiin oo aysan marnaba dagaal la‚Äôaan aheeyn lkn waxaa hortaagnaa Gudoonka Baarlamaanka.
Haduu Gudoomiye Mursal motionka qabtay sidaasna sax ula muqatay waxaan sugeynaa go‚Äôaanka Maxkamadda Sare oo loo gudbin doono. Hayeeshee, wayadaan danbe fulintu weey ka awood badneeyd sharci dejinta welina taasi weey ii muuqataa.
Waxaa adkaa doonta ama aan suuragal aheyn:
In 184 Xildhibaan oo burbur dowladnimao rabto lahelo
2. Xildhibaanada dalka ku sugan oo aan gaareyn 184, u fiirso kalfadhiyadi ugu danbeeyay.
3. Hogaanka Baarlamaanka oo aaan wada socon iyo xukuumadda oo wada socoto. Tasoo keeni karto in ku xigeenka 1 aad isna qabto Motion ka dhan ah Gudoomiyaha Baarlamaanka, sidaasna sheekadu ku noqoto ijiid aan ku jiidee.
4. Gudoomiyaha Maxkamadda sare oo ay u badantahay inuu ka horyimaado soo jeedinta ama Motionka.
5. In arrintaanu ay dhabarjab iyo kala qreybsanaan u keeni karto Paarlamaanka guud ahaan shaqadiisuna hakan doonto Koorom la‚Äôaan.
1. In Madaxweynuha iyo Xukuumadduba aysan shaqadooda ka mashquulin howshoodana qabsadaan
2. In aan qaska iyo jahawareerka lasii badin oo ku xigeenadu aysan iyaguna qaban motion kale oo ka dhan ah Gudoomiyaha Baarlamaanka
3. In wadamada Safaaradahoodu ku milmeen siyaasadda gacan kulul lagu qabto, qaab dowladnimo ahna loola dhaqmo.
Nb. Anigu waxaan hubaa Laba arrimood; In uusan hirgali doonin Motionkaan iyo in Culeeyska ugu weeyn soo wajihi dooni Baarlamaanka (kala qeybsami doono)

Aqoonyahan Mustafe Barud Oo Maanta Xoriyadiisa Dib...
Aqoonyahan Mustafe Barud Oo Maanta Xoriyadiisa Dib U Helay | Oodweynenews.com , Oodweyne News, OODWEYNENEWS
Aqoonyahan Mustafe Barud Oo Maanta Xoriyadiisa Dib U Helay
December 16, 2017 | Published by: Moh
Mustafe Barud oo Maanta Xoriyadiisii Dib Ayuu U helay Ayaa muddo 6 Maalmood ah ku xidhnaa Xabsiga Dhexe ee ku yaala magaaladda Hargeysa , iyadoo aan Ilaa hadda wax maxkamad ah la soo taagin loona sheegin sabaha lagu xidhay.
Ma ahana Wax cusub in Muwaadiniin La iska Xidho, Lana soo daayo isagoon wax cadaalad ah la hor keenin, iyadoo Arintaasina ay horay u dhaawacday Dimuqraadiyadda dalka ka jirta.
Waxaanad halkan hoose ka akhrisataan qoraal uu Mustafe Barud Barta facebook-giisa ku soo qoray markii xabsiga laga sii daayey kaasoo u dhignaa sidan:‚Äî-
‚Äù Galab wacan iyo War farxad leh asxaabta!
Aan ugu horeyn u mahad celiyo Alle oo amarkiisu yahay ka kaliya ee aan baaqan, ciddina baajin karin, laakin aynu Aadame ahaan, sabab uun u yeelno waxa qoraalkiisa ku dhaca. Mar labaada aan u mahad celiy dhamaan akhyaartii, axbaabtii, ehelkii, asxaabtii iyo ciddkaste oo kaalin ka qaadatay soo dayntaydii iyo dhacdaddi xadhigayga.
Mar saddexaad aan si gaara ugu mahad celiyo asxaabtii tirada badnayd ee aan kusoo bartay ayaamihii koobnaa ee aan jeelka ku jiray. Runtii waxa ahaayeen akhyaar aanan ilaabi doonin. Waxa ay dhamaystireen si toos ahna u matalaayeen bulshada inta aan codkoodu ina soo gaadhiin ama aynaan fursadd u siin in aynu waydiino sababta ay xoriyadooda u siistaan qiimaha jaban!!!!!.
Mar afraad ii saamaxa in aan u mahad celiyo saraakiishii, askartii, xeer ilaalintii, garsoorkii iyo dhamaan bahda amniga, caddaaladda iyo garsoorka sidii quruxda badnayd ee ay iila dhaqmeen intii aan la joogay.
Ugu danbayntii saaxiibayaal; waxa qudhiya ee aan ilaa hadda idinla wadaagi karaa waa in aynu sii xoojin doono mihnadeenii siyaasadeed, xoriyatul qawl iyo saxaafadeed. Waa in aynu mar walba la jiri doono runta, sharciga, iyo caddaaladda xataa hadii ay tahay midd inaga in taabanaysa!
Waad mahadsantihiin dhamaantiin! ‚Äú
Aqooonyahan Mustafe Barud

Hogaamiyaha xisbiga Bidixda: Dhacdo tiiraanyo leh ...
Hogaamiyaha xisbiga Bidixda: Dhacdo tiiraanyo leh ayay ahayd - Radio Sweden Somali - Raadiyaha Iswiidhen | Sveriges Radio
Ann-Margarethe Livh oo uu dhaawac ka soo gaaray weerar Muqdisho loogu geeystay
Hogaamiyaha xisbiga Bidixda: Dhacdo tiiraanyo leh ayay ahayd
Margarethe Livh: Dhacdadii iigu naxdinta badnayd
La daabacay torsdag 22 augusti 2013 kl 11.19
Hogaamiyaha xisbiga Bidixda, Jonas Sj√∂sted ayaa shaleyto tacsi ka diray mar uu warramaayay idaacadda la iska daawado ee SVT, sheegayna inuu aad iyo aad uga tiiraanyeeysan yahay geeridii Cabdiraxiin Xasan oo shaleyto lagu diley magaalada Muqdisho.
"Waa dhacdo murugo leh. Waxay maalin madow u tahay xisbiga Bidixda. Cabdi wuxuu ahaa wiil da'yar oo ku dhaqnaa magaalada Istockholm oo booqasho ku tagay Soomaaliya si uu uga qeyb qaato mashruuc uu xisbiga bidixdu waday ee caalami ah. Waxaan la murugooneynaa saaxiibbadiis iyo qaraabadiis. Cabdi wuxuu boos ballaaran ka banneeyay laanta dhallin-yarada ee xisbiga "Ung V√§nster, sida uu sheegay Jonas Sj√∂sted, hogaamiyaha xisbiga Bidixda.
Galab-nimadii shalayto oo weerar lagu qaaday gaari ey saarnaayeen afar ruux eyna ka mid ahaayeen Cabdiraxiin Xasan oo 24-jir ah iyo Anna-Margarethe Livh oo labaduba ka baqooleen magaalada Istockholm ayuu ku geeriyooday Cabdiraxiin Xasan iyo nin soomaali ah ee waardiyeeynayay iyada oo dhanka kale uu dhaawac ka soo gaaray Ann-Margarethe Livh xabadka iyo gacanta oo fiid-nimadii loo duuliyey magaalada Nayroobi si halkaasi loogu siiyo dar-yeel caafimaad.
Ann-Margarethe Livh, oo ka tirsan xisbiga Bidixda, ahna hogaamiyaha xisbiga laantiisa xiriirka caalamiga ayaa booqasho ku tagtay magaalada Muqdisho saddex maalmood hortood iyada oo ey weheliyaan dhallin-yaro ka baqooshay xaafadaha Rinkeby iyo Husby, kolkii weerar lala beegsaday gaari ey saarnayeen, isla-markaana si aan kala go' lahayn xabbado loogu furey. Ann-Margarethe Livh, ayaa sheegtay inay hubaal tahay in weerarkaasi iyaga lagu beegsadey:

WAXAAD TAHAY DUBLIMAASI AAN HADAL KA BIXIN WARAYSI...
WAXAAD TAHAY DUBLIMAASI AAN HADAL KA BIXIN WARAYSI GUDOOMIYAHA WAKIILADA JSL | Toggaherer's Weblog
WAXAAD TAHAY DUBLIMAASI AAN HADAL KA BIXIN WARAYSI GUDOOMIYAHA WAKIILADA JSL
Posted by: toggaherer on: March 15, 2009	In: togaherer
Gudoomiyaha Wakiilladu siduu u arkaa in Golayaasha Baarlamaanku ka arrinsadaan dawlad doorasho dalka gaadhsiisa?
‚Äì Waxa tahay Dublamaasi aan hadal ka bixin, waxaanad ka mid-tahay xisbi is rog-rog badan oo marka la gaadho meel adag u jan-jeedsada dhinaca Xukuumada arrimahaa ka waran?
‚Äì Madaxweyne Rayaale waxaad isugu timaadeen Ingiriiska ka waran kulamadii aad ka wada qayb-gasheen?
Gudoomiyaha Wakiillada: Waraysi gaar ah
Hargeysa -Gudoomiyaha Golaha Wakiillada Somaliland Cabdiraxmaan Maxamed Cabdilaahi (Cabdiraxmaan Ciro) ayaa sheegay in aaney u muuqan caqabad dib doorashada uga riixi karta waqtiga cusub ee Komishanku u mudeeyay, waxaana uu ku taliyey in muranada sharci ee taagan dhameyntooda loo raaco shuruucda dalka Islamarkaana wixii aan sharci ka oolin lagu dhameeyo wadda tashi.
Gudoomiyaha Wakiillada oo Khamiistii doraad ka soo laabtey Socdaal uu ku soo marey dalal ka tirsan qaarada Yurub, waxa uu xalay Wargeyska Ogaal uga waramey socdaalkaasi iyo guud ahaan aragtidiisa ku wajaahan xaalada siyaasadeed ee dalka.
‚ÄúHawlaha qaran ee intii aan Safarka gaarka ah ku jiray noo qabsoomey waxa ka mid ahaa, inaan la kulanay dawladihii aanu wadamadooda tegnay iyo Baarlamaanadooda oo xidhiidh hore naga dhexeeyey oo Baarlamaanka Ingiriisku ka midyihiin, Norwey, Isweden iyo Finland in-taba.
Si guud ayaanu uga waramayney Marxalada Somaliland ku jirto, Doorashooyinka, nabada iyo dhinaca Ictiraafka. Dhamaantoodna wadamadaasi waxay noo sheegeen inay goob joogayaal u soo dirayaan Somaliland doorashadeed. waxa kale oo aad loo daneynayay in doorashadu qabsoonto.‚Äù Sidaas ayuu yidhi Gudoomiyaha Golaha Wakiilladu. Waxana uu intaa ku daray in Madaxweyne Rayaale ay dalka Ingiriiska isku soo gaadheen, balse ka hor intaa Madaxweynu dalkaas u bixin dhawaan uu kulmey Mudanayaal Ingiriiska Baarlamaankiisa ka tirsan oo qadiyada Somaliland u ololeeya. ‚ÄúWaxay noo xaqiijiyeen in Madaxweyne Rayaale Igiriiska Iman doono‚Ä¶taasina ay ka danbeysay balan hore oo Socdaalkii ugu danbeeyey ee Madaxweyne Rayaale ku tago Ingiriiska lagu heshiiyey in dhawrkii Biloodba mar wufuud ka socota Somaliland ay tagaan Ingiriiska ama wufuud Ingiriis ahi ay yimaadaan Somaliland.‚Äù Taasoo uu sheegay inaanay suurta-gelin.
Waxaana uu tilmaamey Gudoomiye Ciro in marti-qaadka Madaxweynaha ee dalka Ingiriisku ahaa mid darajadiisa kor loo qaadey oo ka heer sareeysey socdaaladiisii hore qaarkood. Taasoo uu sheegay inay xidhiidh la lahayd kulanka xog-hayaha arrimaha dibada Ingiriiska dhexmaray.
Markase taas laga yimaado, safarka Madaxweyne Rayaale ku tegay dalka Igiriiska ee ugu danbeeyay, waxa jiray xogo muujineyay in uu la xidhiidho dareenada siyaasadeed ee ka dhashay dib u dhacyada doorashooyinka. Sidaa daraadeed, Gudoomiyaha Wakiillada oo aanu arrintaa wax ka weydiinay waxa uu sheegay in aanu arrintaa waxba ka ogeyn.
‚ÄúMadaxweynaha waanu is aragnay Baarlamaanka markii uu tageyna waan la socday, Xildhibaanada uu la kulmey-na qoladii aan markii hore la kulmay ayay ahaayeen, waxaaney uga warameen uun Safaradii ay Somaliland ku yimaadeen iyo hawlaha ay qabteen ee Somaliland ku saabsan si loo badhitaaro aqoonsigeeda. Hadii ay noqon lahayd in aynu ka mid noqono Barwaaqo sooranka iyo hadii ay ahaan lahayd sidii aynu ugu biiri lahayn Baarlamaanada Aduunka ayay uga warameen waxaaney u rajeeyeen kulanka uu la kulmi doono wasiirka Arrimaha dibada Ingiriisku inuu midha dhal noqdo.‚Äù
Gudoomiyaha waxa la weydiiyey oo kale xaalada siyaasadeed iyo muranada sharci ee dalka ka oogan waqtigan iyo soo jeedinta xisbiga Kulmiye ee la xidhiidha in labada gole ka arrinsadaan waxa laga yeelayo marka la gaadho 6-da bisha soo socota.
‚ÄúHorta, qaran ayaynu nahay, waxaynu leenahay dastuur iyo xeerar. Wixii aynu ka helo shuruucda iyo dastuurka sidooda ayaynu u qaadan doonaa, wixii aynu ka weynana caqligeena ayaynu ku maareyn doonaa.‚Äù Sidaas ayuu yidhi.
Gudoomiye Ciro waxa la sii weydiiyey arragtida iyo doodaha tilmaamaya in marka arrimo noocan ahi yimaadaan ay tahay in labada Gole ee sharci dejintu talo ka gaadhaan, waxaana uu ku jawaabey. ‚ÄúWuu tilmaamayaa Dastuurku in labada Gole ay isu iman karaan, waxaanse ka wadaa uun wax kas-taba aakhirka ha noqoto‚Äôe, in marjac loo noqonayo uu inoo noqdo Dastuurku wixii aynu ka weynana aynu caqligeena la kaashano.‚Äù
Gudoomiyaha Wakiillada waxa la weydiiyey, sida uu u arko walaaca dadka qaar ka qabaan in doorashadu ku qabsoomi karto mudeynta cusub ee Gudiga doorashooyinka ee ah 31-ka May. ‚ÄúWaxaan qabaa waxa ina hor yaala waa arrintaa Serverka oo aan dhamaanin. Carqalad kale oo inaga hor joogta inaynu ilaa 31-ka May qabsano doorashada aniga iima muuqato.‚Äù Sidaas ayuu yidhi Gudoomiyaha Wakiilladu.
Marka laga hadlayo mishiinka kala saaraya dadka isu diiwaan-geliyay doorashada, waxa jira mad-madow ka soo baxay iyo Geeri ka diso ah oo ku timi Gudoomiyihii dhawaan loo magacaabey xilka arrintaasi ka dib markii Gudoomiyihii hore ee Gudiga diiwaan-gelinta xilka laga qaadey.
Sidaa darteed, Maadaama Gudoomiyaha Wakiilladu ka mid-yahay masuuliyiinta ugu sar-sareysa ee dalka waxa la weydiiyay arragtidiisa arrintaa ku wajahan iyo sida looga bixi karo caqabadaha taagan. Hase ahaatee, Gudoomiye Ciro arrintaas wuu ka gal-gashay. Waxana uu sheegey in Gole ahaan ay la soconayaan geediga hawsha doorshada, balse waxa uu tilaamay in arrintaas xilkeedu saaran-yahay cida gacanta ku heysa.
Gudoomiye Cabdiraxmaan waa dublamaasi Af-gaaban oo aan bixin jawaabo waafiya oo ku saabsan arrimaha saxaafadu wax ka weydiiso, waxana uu ka mid-yahay Xisbiga UCID oo loo arrko xisbi marka arrimo addag la isku qabto u jan-jeedhsada dhinaca Xukuumada, dadka qaar-na waxa ay u tiriyaan Cabdiraxmaan inuu noqon doono mustaqbalka Gudoomiyaha xisbiga ee kala wareegaya Faysal.
Su‚Äôaal arrimahaas shaqsi iyo Xisbinimo isugu dhafan oo la weydiiyey Gudoomiyaha Wakiiladu waxa uu kaga jawaabey ‚ÄúAnnigu ma jecli inaan Xisbiga UCID ku hadlo magaciisa..waa dhab xisbiga ayaan ka tirsanahay, madaxdiisa ayaan ka mid ahay. Tan gudoomiyahana marka wakhtigeedu yimaado ayaan ka jawaabi doonaa. Ta mawaaqiifta Xisbiga waxay illa tahay inaad xisbiga weydiiso.‚Äù
Gudoomiyaha Wakiillada waxa la weydiiyey oo kale arragti ahaan in uu aaminsan-yahay in la sameeyo dawlad ku meel-gaadh ah oo lixda bisha Afraad ka dib xilka la wareegta dalkana doorasho gaadhsiisa iyo in kale? ‚ÄúWaxay illa tahay inay jiraan hawlo ka horeeya 6-da April oo taas Severku ka mid-tahay oo laga yaabo in xalkooduba ka soo horeeyo. markaa waxay illa tahay aynu taas ka dhur-sugno oo yeynaan ka hor dhicin arrintaas.‚Äù

Ciidamada AMISOM oo Qarax lagula eegtay Muqdisho ‚Äî Mareeg.com - is independent news website. Read All Africa news,Somalia news headlines, photos and videos on Somalia. Track breaking Somalia news & analysis
By John Snow	 Last updated Feb 17, 2019
Qaraxaan ayaa waxa uu ka dhacay agagaarka Ex-kontorool Balcad ee Wadada Warshadaha gobolkan Banaadir,waxaana sida lasheegay lala eegtay Ciidamoka tirsan kuwa Midowga Afrika ee AMISOM.
Dad aan lahadalnay ayaa Risaala waxa ay u sheegeen in Miinada nooca dhulka lagu aaso ah lala eegtay kolonyo ka tirsan Ciidamada AMISOM oo wadada ku socdaalayay,isla markaana ay maqlayeen jugta qaraxa.
Sidoo kale wararka ayaa waxa ay intaasi ku darayaan in qaraxa kadib ciidamada AMISOM ay rideen rasaas farabadan,hayeeshee waxaa weli la ogeyn khasaaraha qaraxa Ciidamada AMISOM kasoo gaaray iyo in ay dad rayid ah wax ku noqdeen rasaastii ay fureen.
Waxaa haatan hakad ku jira isku-socodka dadka iyo Gaadiidka ee Wadada Warshadaha gaar ahaan agagaarka Ex-koontorool Balcad oo kolonyo ka tirsan Ciidamada AMISOM qarax lagu laeegtay.

Meejar Jenaraal Kinfee Daanyaw to'annoo jala oolan...
Meejar Jenaraal Kinfee Daanyaw to'annoo jala oolanii Finfinnee dhufaa jiru - BBC News Afaan Oromoo
https://www.bbc.com/afaanoromoo/oduu-46190645?ocid=socialflow_facebook
Daarektarri Olaanaa duraanii Korporeeshinii Sibiilaafi Injiinaringii (MeTEC) Meejar Janaraal Kinfee Daanyaw to'annaa jala oolan.
Erga to'annaa jala oolfamanii booda gara Finfinnee fidamuu isaanii miidiyaan biyya keessaa gabaasanii jiru.
Aanga'aan kun naannoo Tigiraay bakka Humaraa jedhamutti wayita to'annoo jala oolchan miidiyaan biyyaalessaa ETV'n kallattiin tamsaasee jira.
Hojii Korporeeshinichaa waliin walqabateen kan shakkaman Daarekteerichi gama Lixa Tigiraayitti kan argamtu Baataar bakka jedhamtutti tumsa hawwaasaafi humna ittisaatiin ture kan to'annaa jala oolan.
Guyyaa kaleessaa Abbaan Alangaa Mootummaa Federaalaa saamicha maallaqaa guddaatiin kan shakkaman gaggeessitoota ol aanoo MeTEC namoota 27 akkasumas ogeessota to'annoo jala oolfamuu ibsa kennee ture.
Akka Abbaan Alangaa Federaalaa Kaleessa jedhetti 'METEC' birrii biiliyoona 37 oliin dorgommii caalbaasii malee biyya alaatii bittaa raawwateera.
Bittaan biyya keessaas dhaabbilee hoogganoota 'METEC' waliin hidhata michummaa fi firummaa qaban irraa caal-baasii malee raawwatame jedhan Obbo Birhaanuun.

KEYDMEDIA - First Modern Somali News & Video Websi...
KEYDMEDIA - First Modern Somali News & Video Website - Maqaallo - MA RUNBAA IN AY XIRIIR LEEYIHIIN DAHABSHIIL IYO KOOXDA GODANE?
Friday 29 October 2010 | KON
Burburkii Soomaaliya ee 1991-dii wixii ka danbeeyay Dalka waxaa ka hirgalay howla horumar lagu sheegay laakiin si kale marka loo eego dhibaato inteeda la eg lagala kulmay.
Tartan xaasidnimo ku saleysan oo u dhaxeeya shirkadaha u abaabulan qaabka qabiil ee sheega in ay ganacsi horumar leh dalka ka hirgaliyeen ayaa shacabka marasta ah ee dagaalada, abaaraha iyo dhibaatooyinka kale ay la dageen waxa ay ka kulmeen caqabad balaaran.
Shirkadda Dahabshiil sida ku xusan profile-keeda waxaa ay dhaq dhaqaaqa ganacsi bilowaday 1970-kii waxaana mudda badan ay ku shaqeyneysay nidaam qarsoodi ah oo aan sharci aheyn, laakiin wixii ka danbeeyay burburkii ayey la soo shaac baxday dar dar xoog leh.
Soomaalida dhexdeeda waa arrin iska caada ah in lagu arko qorshaha ku dhisan qabiilka iyo qabiileysiga, waxaana shirkadan ay mudadii ay jirtay dhex maquuraneysay nidaamka ku saleysan qabiileysiga, wallow ay dhanka kale ay gacaan saar la leedahay sirdoonka caalamka.
Walaac kii ugu xooganaa waxa uu la darsay Dahabshiil bartamihii sanadkan kadib markii Shirkada Hormuud oo ku caan aheyd bixinta adeegyada kale duwan ee telfoonka ay Dalka geysay nidaam dunida laga adeegsado kaasoo ah Mobile money transfer, waxaana adeegan culeys uu ku keenay adeegii xawaaladeed ee Dahabshiil.
Soomaalidu waxay tiraahdaa Bahal Ceyriin ma daayo nina caadadii ma baajo, taasoo ay uga gol leedahay Soomaalida in aanu Shaqsina dhaqankiisa is doorineyn, Shirkad xawaaladeedkan waxa ay ka baxday nidaamkii ku saleysan tartanka dhaqaale, waxaana ay magansatay awood beeleed.
Axmed Cabdi Aw-Max‚Äôud Godane waxa ay heeb wadaag yihiin madax sare oo ka tirsan Shirkadda, waxaana taasi ay fududeysay in Waraqad digniin ah ay ka soo saarto kooxda Godane adeegii Hormuud ee Mobile Money transfer oo shirkadaasi ay uga magac dartay ‚ÄúZAAD‚Äù oo afka Soomaaliga marka loo rogo ah Sahay.
Warqadda kooxda Godane ay ku diiday isticmaalka adeega ZAAD ayaa waxa ay soo baxday bartamihii bishan waxaana ku xardhanaa erayo ay ka muuqdaan dagaal qabiil iyo nidaam lagu difaacayo dano beeleed isla markaana beel kale lagu curyaaminayo, waxaa lagu xusay warqadda in adeegaasi loogu shaqeeyo Maraykan ama Yahuud isla markaana la farayo shirkadda iyo macaamiishaba in muddo ku siman 3 bilood ay ku soo afjaraaan adeegsigiisa.
Hadaba aynu Eegno xiriirka Sirdoonka Caalamka iyo Dahabshiil
Xogo la helay waxa ay sheegayaan in Shirkaddan ay ka talaabtan sharci ahaan nidaamka xawaaladaha caalamka loo jaangooyay, kaasoo ah in xawaalad aanay awoodin kala gudbinta in ka badan 2 Milyan oo Doolar, laakiin shirkan waxa ay xawishaa lacagaha ay adeegsadaan sirdoonka Caalamka kuwaasoo cadad ahaan aan la qiyaasi Karin, waxaana taasi ay muujineysaa in xiriir adag oo ay sirdoonka la leeyihiin inuu jiro.
Dhanka kale shirkadani waa tan lagu xawilo lacagaha madax furashada loo siiyo burcad badeeda caalamka, waxaana taasi sahlay shirkadda oo gacan saar la leh mukhaadaraadka aduunka sida kuwa fura wada hadalada u dhaxeeya burcad badeeda iyo milkiilayaasha Maraakiibta la qafaasho.
Dad badan oo isticmaalka adeega ZAAD ee Hormuud la jaanqaaday waxay eedeyn aan ka fiirsi laheyn dusha uga tuuraan kooxda GODANE oo ay la tahay iyagu in ay iska maageen shirkadda Hormuud isla markaana adeega ZAAD ay iska joojiyeen, laakiin waxaa hareer marsan shacabka in yabooh lacageed oo balaaran in la siiyay kooxda, isla markaana uu jiro dhalasho iyo qaraabo-nimo hoose. Oo ka dhaxeysa kooxda iyo Shirkadda
Soo shaac bixii talaabada lagu soo saaray amarka lagu diiday adeegii ZAAD waxa ay noqotay furaha soo ifbixidda xiriirka ka dhaxeeya Shirkadda Dahabshiil ee magaca ganacsi huwan iyo kooxda Godane oo iminka ka dagaalanta guud ahaan gayiga Soomaaliya.
Waa suurta gal in dad badan oo macaamiil lalahaa shirkaddasi isla markaana ku keedsan jiray lacago in ay ka aamin baxaan sabab la xiriirta iyagoo cabsi ka muujnaya in lacagahooda ay ka mid noqdaan kuwa lagu hurinayo dagaalada ka socda Dalka ee marasta lagu dhibaateynayo.
Inkastoo shirkada ganacsi oo badan isla markaana maalka shacabka ku taajiray la aaminsanyahay in ay ku lugleeyihiin dhibataada dalka ka socota,hadana tani waxay noqotay tii ugu horeysay ee cadeyn buuxda loo helo isla markaana ka ganbanweysay laablakacnimada ku dhisan awooda qabiil.
Dr. Warsame Ali (Fiisiko) - .(JavaScript must be enabled to view this email address)
